        <script>
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // CORE 1: Web Audio API Synthesizer (MND Pro Engine)
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            let proCtx = null;
            let masterVol, subBassGain, distNode, lowpassFilter, analyserNode;
            let canvasPro, ctxPro, animFrame;
            let engineOn = false;

            // Audio Context Initialization (Must be triggered by user action)
            async function toggleAudioEngine() {
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                const btn = document.getElementById('enginePwrBtn');
                const led = document.getElementById('enginePowerLed');
                const studioWrap = document.getElementById('mndStudioEngine');

                if(!engineOn) {
                    try {
                        const AudioContext = window.AudioContext || window.webkitAudioContext;
                        proCtx = new AudioContext();
                        
                        // Build Audio Routing Graph
                        buildAudioGraph();
                        
                        // Setup Canvas Visualizer
                        setupCanvas();
                        drawOscilloscope();

                        engineOn = true;
                        led.classList.add('on');
                        btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-power-off"></i> SYSTEM ONLINE';
                        btn.style.color = '#00ff00';
                        btn.style.borderColor = '#00ff00';
                        btn.style.background = 'rgba(0,255,0,0.1)';
                        studioWrap.style.boxShadow = '0 30px 60px rgba(0,0,0,0.9), inset 0 2px 5px rgba(255,255,255,0.05), inset 0 -5px 15px rgba(0,229,255,0.3)';

                        showToast("MND Core Audio Engine Initialized.");
                    } catch(e) {
                        alert("Audio processing not supported in this browser environment.");
                    }
                } else {
                    if(proCtx) await proCtx.close();
                    engineOn = false;
                    led.classList.remove('on');
                    btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-power-off"></i> BOOT ENGINE';
                    btn.style.color = 'var(--accent-red)';
                    btn.style.borderColor = 'var(--accent-red)';
                    btn.style.background = 'transparent';
                    studioWrap.style.boxShadow = '';
                    if(animFrame) cancelAnimationFrame(animFrame);
                    ctxPro.clearRect(0, 0, canvasPro.width, canvasPro.height);
                }
            }

            function buildAudioGraph() {
                // 1. Distortion Node (WaveShaper curve)
                distNode = proCtx.createWaveShaper();
                distNode.curve = makeDistortionCurve(0); // initial 0
                distNode.oversample = '4x';

                // 2. Lowpass Filter
                lowpassFilter = proCtx.createBiquadFilter();
                lowpassFilter.type = 'lowpass';
                lowpassFilter.frequency.value = 20000; // Wide open initially

                // 3. Sub Bass Enhancer (Parallel path)
                subBassGain = proCtx.createGain();
                subBassGain.gain.value = 1.0;
                
                // 4. Analyser for Canvas
                analyserNode = proCtx.createAnalyser();
                analyserNode.fftSize = 2048; // High res for oscilloscope

                // 5. Master Volume
                masterVol = proCtx.createGain();
                masterVol.gain.value = 0.8; // default 80%

                // Connect the chain: Source -> Distortion -> Filter -> Master -> Analyser -> Speakers
                // Sub Bass routing is handled per sound
                distNode.connect(lowpassFilter);
                lowpassFilter.connect(masterVol);
                subBassGain.connect(masterVol);
                masterVol.connect(analyserNode);
                analyserNode.connect(proCtx.destination);
            }

            // Math function for heavy distortion
            function makeDistortionCurve(amount) {
                const k = typeof amount === 'number' ? amount : 50;
                const n_samples = 44100;
                const curve = new Float32Array(n_samples);
                const deg = Math.PI / 180;
                for (let i = 0; i < n_samples; ++i) {
                    const x = i * 2 / n_samples - 1;
                    curve[i] = (3 + k) * x * 20 * deg / (Math.PI + k * Math.abs(x));
                }
                return curve;
            }

            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // CORE 2: Interactive SVG Knobs Logic
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            const knobs = document.querySelectorAll('.knob-base');
            let activeKnob = null;
            let startY = 0;
            let currentVal = 0;

            knobs.forEach(knob => {
                // Mouse Events
                knob.addEventListener('mousedown', (e) => {
                    activeKnob = knob;
                    startY = e.clientY;
                    currentVal = parseInt(knob.getAttribute('data-value'));
                    document.body.style.cursor = 'grabbing';
                    e.preventDefault(); // Prevent text selection
                });

                // Touch Events
                knob.addEventListener('touchstart', (e) => {
                    activeKnob = knob;
                    startY = e.touches[0].clientY;
                    currentVal = parseInt(knob.getAttribute('data-value'));
                    document.body.style.cursor = 'grabbing';
                }, {passive: false});
            });

            document.addEventListener('mousemove', handleKnobMove);
            document.addEventListener('touchmove', (e) => {
                if(activeKnob) {
                    e.preventDefault(); // Stop scrolling while turning knob
                    handleKnobMove({clientY: e.touches[0].clientY});
                }
            }, {passive: false});

            document.addEventListener('mouseup', () => { activeKnob = null; document.body.style.cursor = 'default'; });
            document.addEventListener('touchend', () => { activeKnob = null; document.body.style.cursor = 'default'; });

            function handleKnobMove(e) {
                if (!activeKnob) return;
                
                const min = parseInt(activeKnob.getAttribute('data-min'));
                const max = parseInt(activeKnob.getAttribute('data-max'));
                
                // Calculate delta (moving mouse UP increases value)
                const deltaY = startY - e.clientY; 
                let newVal = currentVal + (deltaY * 2); // sensitivity
                
                // Clamp values
                if (newVal < min) newVal = min;
                if (newVal > max) newVal = max;
                
                // Update DOM
                activeKnob.setAttribute('data-value', newVal);
                const dial = activeKnob.querySelector('.knob-dial');
                dial.style.transform = `rotate(${newVal}deg)`;
                
                // Apply to Audio Engine
                applyKnobToAudio(activeKnob.id, newVal, min, max);
                
                // Update start position for smooth continuous drag
                startY = e.clientY;
                currentVal = newVal;
            }

            function applyKnobToAudio(knobId, val, min, max) {
                if(!engineOn) return;
                
                // Normalize value between 0.0 and 1.0
                const norm = (val - min) / (max - min);

                switch(knobId) {
                    case 'knobMaster':
                        masterVol.gain.setTargetAtTime(norm * 1.5, proCtx.currentTime, 0.05);
                        break;
                    case 'knobBass':
                        // Sub bass gain multiplier (0 to 3)
                        subBassGain.gain.setTargetAtTime(norm * 3.0, proCtx.currentTime, 0.05);
                        break;
                    case 'knobDist':
                        // Distortion amount (0 to 100)
                        distNode.curve = makeDistortionCurve(norm * 100);
                        break;
                    case 'knobFilter':
                        // Exponential frequency map (20Hz to 20000Hz)
                        const minFreq = 40;
                        const maxFreq = 20000;
                        // Math.exp yields a natural sounding sweep
                        const freq = minFreq * Math.pow(maxFreq / minFreq, norm);
                        lowpassFilter.frequency.setTargetAtTime(freq, proCtx.currentTime, 0.05);
                        break;
                }
            }

            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // CORE 3: Canvas Oscilloscope (Real-time Waveform)
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            function setupCanvas() {
                canvasPro = document.getElementById('mndCanvasPro');
                ctxPro = canvasPro.getContext('2d');
                
                // Handle high-DPI displays cleanly
                const dpr = window.devicePixelRatio || 1;
                const rect = canvasPro.getBoundingClientRect();
                canvasPro.width = rect.width * dpr;
                canvasPro.height = rect.height * dpr;
                ctxPro.scale(dpr, dpr);
            }

            function drawOscilloscope() {
                if(!engineOn) return;
                animFrame = requestAnimationFrame(drawOscilloscope);

                const bufferLength = analyserNode.frequencyBinCount;
                const dataArray = new Uint8Array(bufferLength);
                analyserNode.getByteTimeDomainData(dataArray); // Get Waveform, not Frequency

                // CSS width/height
                const w = canvasPro.clientWidth;
                const h = canvasPro.clientHeight;

                // Motion blur clear
                ctxPro.fillStyle = 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3)';
                ctxPro.fillRect(0, 0, w, h);

                ctxPro.lineWidth = 2;
                ctxPro.strokeStyle = '#00e5ff';
                ctxPro.beginPath();

                const sliceWidth = w * 1.0 / bufferLength;
                let x = 0;

                for (let i = 0; i < bufferLength; i++) {
                    const v = dataArray[i] / 128.0; // 128 is center
                    const y = v * h / 2;

                    if (i === 0) { ctxPro.moveTo(x, y); } 
                    else { ctxPro.lineTo(x, y); }
                    x += sliceWidth;
                }

                ctxPro.lineTo(w, h / 2);
                ctxPro.stroke();
            }

            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // CORE 4: Synthesis Pad Logic (Producing the sounds)
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            function engineRelease(element) {
                element.classList.remove('active-state');
            }

            function enginePlay(sound, element) {
                if(!engineOn) {
                    showToast("⚠️ Power on the Engine first!");
                    // Shake the power button to alert user
                    const pwrBtn = document.getElementById('enginePwrBtn');
                    pwrBtn.style.animation = 'heavyBassShake 0.4s';
                    setTimeout(() => pwrBtn.style.animation = '', 400);
                    return;
                }
                
                element.classList.add('active-state');
                if(navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate(20);
                
                const t = proCtx.currentTime;
                
                switch(sound) {
                    case 'sub808':
                        // Pure low sine wave with slow decay
                        const o8 = proCtx.createOscillator();
                        const g8 = proCtx.createGain();
                        o8.type = 'sine'; o8.frequency.setValueAtTime(45, t);
                        // Pitch bend
                        o8.frequency.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(30, t + 1.5);
                        o8.connect(g8); g8.connect(subBassGain); // Route to heavy bass channel
                        g8.gain.setValueAtTime(1, t);
                        g8.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, t + 1.5);
                        o8.start(t); o8.stop(t + 1.5);
                        break;

                    case 'snare2':
                        // Punchy noise burst
                        const nBuf = proCtx.createBuffer(1, proCtx.sampleRate * 0.5, proCtx.sampleRate);
                        const nData = nBuf.getChannelData(0);
                        for (let i = 0; i < nBuf.length; i++) nData[i] = Math.random() * 2 - 1;
                        
                        const nSrc = proCtx.createBufferSource();
                        nSrc.buffer = nBuf;
                        const nFilt = proCtx.createBiquadFilter();
                        nFilt.type = 'highpass'; nFilt.frequency.value = 1000;
                        const nGain = proCtx.createGain();
                        nGain.gain.setValueAtTime(1, t);
                        nGain.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.01, t + 0.2);
                        
                        nSrc.connect(nFilt); nFilt.connect(nGain); nGain.connect(distNode);
                        nSrc.start(t);
                        break;
                        
                    case 'laserA':
                        const lA = proCtx.createOscillator();
                        const lG = proCtx.createGain();
                        lA.type = 'sawtooth';
                        lA.frequency.setValueAtTime(1500, t);
                        lA.frequency.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(100, t + 0.3);
                        lA.connect(lG); lG.connect(distNode);
                        lG.gain.setValueAtTime(0.8, t);
                        lG.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.01, t + 0.3);
                        lA.start(t); lA.stop(t + 0.3);
                        break;
                        
                    case 'djHorn':
                        // Multi-oscillator dissonant chord to simulate stadium horn
                        [300, 340, 380].forEach(freq => {
                            const o = proCtx.createOscillator();
                            const g = proCtx.createGain();
                            o.type = 'square';
                            o.frequency.setValueAtTime(freq, t);
                            o.frequency.linearRampToValueAtTime(freq * 1.2, t + 0.1);
                            o.frequency.linearRampToValueAtTime(freq, t + 0.4);
                            o.connect(g); g.connect(distNode);
                            g.gain.setValueAtTime(0, t);
                            g.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0.4, t + 0.05);
                            g.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.01, t + 0.5);
                            o.start(t); o.stop(t + 0.5);
                        });
                        break;
                        
                    // Fallback simple beep for unmapped pads to ensure feedback
                    default:
                        const fb = proCtx.createOscillator();
                        const fG = proCtx.createGain();
                        fb.frequency.value = 880;
                        fb.connect(fG); fG.connect(masterVol);
                        fG.gain.setValueAtTime(0.5, t);
                        fG.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.01, t + 0.1);
                        fb.start(t); fb.stop(t + 0.1);
                }
            }

            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // CORE 5: 3D Holographic Carousel Engine
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            const scene = document.getElementById('holoScene');
            const faces = document.querySelectorAll('.holo-face');
            const faceCount = faces.length; // 8
            const theta = 360 / faceCount; // 45 degrees
            
            // Calculate radius dynamically based on face width to ensure perfect octagon
            // Formula: r = (width / 2) / tan(PI / n)
            // Assuming face width is roughly 320px
            const radius = Math.round((320 / 2) / Math.tan(Math.PI / faceCount));
            
            let currIndex = 0;
            let holoAutoPlay = null;

            // Position the faces in 3D space
            faces.forEach((face, i) => {
                const angle = theta * i;
                face.style.transform = `rotateY(${angle}deg) translateZ(${radius}px)`;
            });

            function updateHoloRotation() {
                const angle = theta * currIndex * -1;
                scene.style.transform = `translateZ(${-radius}px) rotateY(${angle}deg)`;
            }

            function rotateCarousel(dir) {
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                currIndex += dir;
                updateHoloRotation();
                
                // If manually interacting, reset auto-play timer
                if(holoAutoPlay) {
                    clearInterval(holoAutoPlay);
                    startHoloAutoPlay();
                }
            }

            function startHoloAutoPlay() {
                holoAutoPlay = setInterval(() => {
                    currIndex++;
                    updateHoloRotation();
                }, 3000);
                document.getElementById('ccAutoBtn').innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-pause"></i>';
            }

            function toggleAutoRotate() {
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                if(holoAutoPlay) {
                    clearInterval(holoAutoPlay);
                    holoAutoPlay = null;
                    document.getElementById('ccAutoBtn').innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-play"></i>';
                } else {
                    startHoloAutoPlay();
                }
            }

            // Initialize position and start auto-play
            updateHoloRotation();
            startHoloAutoPlay();

            // Draggable Carousel Logic (Touch & Mouse)
            let hStartX = 0;
            let isHoloDragging = false;

            scene.addEventListener('mousedown', (e) => {
                isHoloDragging = true;
                hStartX = e.clientX;
                if(holoAutoPlay) clearInterval(holoAutoPlay);
                scene.style.transition = 'none'; // remove transition for smooth dragging
            });

            document.addEventListener('mousemove', (e) => {
                if(!isHoloDragging) return;
                const hDeltaX = e.clientX - hStartX;
                const baseAngle = theta * currIndex * -1;
                // Calculate partial rotation based on drag distance
                const dragAngle = baseAngle + (hDeltaX * 0.2); 
                scene.style.transform = `translateZ(${-radius}px) rotateY(${dragAngle}deg)`;
            });

            document.addEventListener('mouseup', (e) => {
                if(!isHoloDragging) return;
                isHoloDragging = false;
                const hDeltaX = e.clientX - hStartX;
                scene.style.transition = 'transform 0.6s cubic-bezier(0.25, 1, 0.5, 1)';
                
                // Determine if drag was far enough to snap to next face
                if(hDeltaX > 50) currIndex--;
                else if(hDeltaX < -50) currIndex++;
                
                updateHoloRotation();
                if(document.getElementById('ccAutoBtn').innerHTML.includes('pause')) startHoloAutoPlay();
            });

            // Touch support for Mobile
            scene.addEventListener('touchstart', (e) => {
                isHoloDragging = true; hStartX = e.touches[0].clientX;
                if(holoAutoPlay) clearInterval(holoAutoPlay);
                scene.style.transition = 'none';
            }, {passive:true});
            scene.addEventListener('touchmove', (e) => {
                if(!isHoloDragging) return;
                const hDeltaX = e.touches[0].clientX - hStartX;
                const baseAngle = theta * currIndex * -1;
                const dragAngle = baseAngle + (hDeltaX * 0.3); 
                scene.style.transform = `translateZ(${-radius}px) rotateY(${dragAngle}deg)`;
            }, {passive:true});
            scene.addEventListener('touchend', (e) => {
                if(!isHoloDragging) return;
                isHoloDragging = false;
                const hDeltaX = e.changedTouches[0].clientX - hStartX; // changedTouches for touchend
                scene.style.transition = 'transform 0.6s cubic-bezier(0.25, 1, 0.5, 1)';
                if(hDeltaX > 40) currIndex--; else if(hDeltaX < -40) currIndex++;
                updateHoloRotation();
                if(document.getElementById('ccAutoBtn').innerHTML.includes('pause')) startHoloAutoPlay();
            });
        </script>

        <style>
            .pano-viewer-wrapper {
                width: 100%;
                height: 400px;
                border-radius: var(--border-radius-lg);
                border: 2px solid var(--gold-primary);
                margin-top: 60px;

                cursor: grab;
            }
            .pano-viewer-wrapper:active { cursor: grabbing; }

            /* The ultra-wide panning background */
            .pano-image {
                position: absolute;
                top: 0; left: 0;
                width: 200%; /* Wider than container to allow panning */
                height: 100%;
                background-image: url('https://i.postimg.cc/pXx5fqGQ/image_fac9be10.png');
                background-size: cover;
                background-position: center center;
                transition: transform 0.1s ease-out;

            .pano-hud {
                position: absolute;

                background: rgba(0,0,0,0.6);
                backdrop-filter: blur(10px);
                border: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.2);
                border-radius: 30px;
                padding: 10px 25px;
                display: flex;
                align-items: center;
                gap: 15px;
                z-index: 10;
                pointer-events: none;
            }
            .pano-hud i { color: #fff; font-size: 20px; animation: slideLeftRight 2s infinite ease-in-out alternate; }
            .pano-hud span { color: var(--gold-primary); font-family: 'Rajdhani'; font-weight: bold; letter-spacing: 2px; }

            @keyframes slideLeftRight {
                0% { transform: translateX(-5px); }
                100% { transform: translateX(5px); }
            }

            /* Viewfinder Center Target */
            .pano-target {
                position: absolute;
                top: 50%; left: 50%;
                transform: translate(-50%, -50%);
                width: 40px; height: 40px;
                border: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.3);
                border-radius: 50%;
                pointer-events: none;
                z-index: 5;
            }
            .pano-target::after {
                content: ''; position: absolute; top: 50%; left: 50%; transform: translate(-50%, -50%);
                width: 4px; height: 4px; background: var(--accent-red); border-radius: 50%;
            }
        </style>

        <div class="showcase-container reveal-on-scroll">
            <h2 class="section-label-pro"><i class="fas fa-vr-cardboard"></i> 360° VIP PANDAL TOUR</h2>
            <p style="text-align: center; color: var(--text-sub); font-family: 'Outfit'; font-size: 13px; margin-top:-15px;">Drag to explore the structural elegance of our luxury setups.</p>

            <div class="pano-viewer-wrapper" id="panoContainer">
                <div class="pano-image" id="panoImage"></div>
                <div class="pano-target"></div>
                <div class="pano-hud">
                    <i class="fas fa-hand-pointer"></i>
                    <span>DRAG TO PAN</span>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>

        <script>
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // BB. Custom Touch/Mouse Drag Engine for Dream Crafter
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            const stageCanvas = document.getElementById('stageCanvas');
            const inventoryItems = document.querySelectorAll('.drag-item');
            let currentTotalBudget = 0;
            const budgetDisplay = document.getElementById('builderTotal');

            let activeDragItem = null;
            let offsetX = 0, offsetY = 0;
            let isDraggingNew = false; // Is it coming from palette or already on stage?

            // 1. Handle items in the Palette
            inventoryItems.forEach(item => {
                item.addEventListener('touchstart', handleDragStart, {passive: false});
                item.addEventListener('mousedown', handleDragStart);
            });

            function handleDragStart(e) {
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                if(e.type === 'touchstart') e.preventDefault(); // Prevent scrolling

                const touch = e.type === 'touchstart' ? e.touches[0] : e;
                const target = e.currentTarget;

                // Create a clone to drag if it's from the palette
                if (target.classList.contains('drag-item')) {
                    isDraggingNew = true;
                    activeDragItem = document.createElement('div');
                    activeDragItem.className = 'placed-item';
                    activeDragItem.innerHTML = target.querySelector('i').outerHTML;
                    activeDragItem.dataset.price = target.dataset.price;
                    
                    // Attach movement listeners to the new clone
                    activeDragItem.addEventListener('touchstart', handleDragStart, {passive: false});
                    activeDragItem.addEventListener('mousedown', handleDragStart);

                    document.body.appendChild(activeDragItem); // Temporarily append to body to float over everything
                    
                    // Center clone on finger
                    activeDragItem.style.left = (touch.pageX - 25) + 'px';
                    activeDragItem.style.top = (touch.pageY - 25) + 'px';
                } else {
                    // Moving an already placed item
                    isDraggingNew = false;
                    activeDragItem = target;
                    const rect = activeDragItem.getBoundingClientRect();
                    offsetX = touch.clientX - rect.left;
                    offsetY = touch.clientY - rect.top;
                }
            }

            // Global Move Handlers
            document.addEventListener('touchmove', handleDragMove, {passive: false});
            document.addEventListener('mousemove', handleDragMove);

            function handleDragMove(e) {
                if (!activeDragItem) return;
                e.preventDefault(); // Stop scrolling

                const touch = e.type === 'touchmove' ? e.touches[0] : e;
                
                if(isDraggingNew) {
                    // Moving newly spawned clone
                    activeDragItem.style.left = (touch.pageX - 25) + 'px';
                    activeDragItem.style.top = (touch.pageY - 25) + 'px';
                } else {
                    // Moving existing item within canvas bounds
                    const canvasRect = stageCanvas.getBoundingClientRect();
                    let newX = touch.clientX - canvasRect.left - offsetX;
                    let newY = touch.clientY - canvasRect.top - offsetY;

                    // Boundaries
                    if(newX < 0) newX = 0;
                    if(newY < 0) newY = 0;
                    if(newX > canvasRect.width - 50) newX = canvasRect.width - 50;
                    if(newY > canvasRect.height - 50) newY = canvasRect.height - 50;

                    activeDragItem.style.left = newX + 'px';
                    activeDragItem.style.top = newY + 'px';
                }
            }

            // Global End Handlers
            document.addEventListener('touchend', handleDragEnd);
            document.addEventListener('mouseup', handleDragEnd);

            function handleDragEnd(e) {
                if (!activeDragItem) return;

                if (isDraggingNew) {
                    const touch = e.type === 'touchend' ? e.changedTouches[0] : e;
                    const canvasRect = stageCanvas.getBoundingClientRect();

                    // Check if dropped inside canvas
                    if (
                        touch.clientX > canvasRect.left &&
                        touch.clientX < canvasRect.right &&
                        touch.clientY > canvasRect.top &&
                        touch.clientY < canvasRect.bottom
                    ) {
                        // Successful drop
                        if(navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate(10);
                        
                        // Append to canvas and adjust coordinates relative to canvas
                        stageCanvas.appendChild(activeDragItem);
                        const newX = touch.clientX - canvasRect.left - 25;
                        const newY = touch.clientY - canvasRect.top - 25;
                        activeDragItem.style.left = newX + 'px';
                        activeDragItem.style.top = newY + 'px';
                        
                        // Update Budget
                        const price = parseInt(activeDragItem.dataset.price);
                        currentTotalBudget += price;
                        animateBudgetVal(currentTotalBudget);

                    } else {
                        // Dropped outside, destroy clone
                        activeDragItem.remove();
                    }
                }
                
                activeDragItem = null;
                isDraggingNew = false;
            }

            function clearStage() {
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                const items = stageCanvas.querySelectorAll('.placed-item');
                items.forEach(item => {
                    item.style.transform = 'scale(0)';
                    setTimeout(()=> item.remove(), 300);
                });
                currentTotalBudget = 0;
                animateBudgetVal(0);
            }

            function animateBudgetVal(finalVal) {
                const startVal = parseInt(budgetDisplay.innerText.replace('₹', '').replace(/,/g, '')) || 0;
                const duration = 400;
                let startTime = null;

                function step(timestamp) {
                    if (!startTime) startTime = timestamp;
                    const progress = Math.min((timestamp - startTime) / duration, 1);
                    const current = Math.floor(progress * (finalVal - startVal) + startVal);
                    budgetDisplay.innerText = `₹${current.toLocaleString()}`;
                    if (progress < 1) {
                        window.requestAnimationFrame(step);
                    }
                }
                window.requestAnimationFrame(step);
                
                budgetDisplay.style.transform = 'scale(1.1)';
                setTimeout(() => budgetDisplay.style.transform = 'scale(1)', 200);
            }

            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // CC. 360 Panoramic Engine Logic
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            const panoContainer = document.getElementById('panoContainer');
            const panoImage = document.getElementById('panoImage');
            
            let isPanoDragging = false;
            let panoStartX = 0;
            let currentTranslateX = 0;
            // The image is 200% width, so max translation is -50%
            const minTranslate = -50; 
            const maxTranslate = 0;

            panoContainer.addEventListener('mousedown', pDragStart);
            panoContainer.addEventListener('touchstart', pDragStart, {passive: true});

            function pDragStart(e) {
                isPanoDragging = true;
                panoStartX = e.type === 'touchstart' ? e.touches[0].clientX : e.clientX;
                panoImage.style.transition = 'none'; // Instant follow finger
            }

            window.addEventListener('mousemove', pDragMove);
            window.addEventListener('touchmove', pDragMove, {passive: true});

            function pDragMove(e) {
                if(!isPanoDragging) return;
                const clientX = e.type === 'touchmove' ? e.touches[0].clientX : e.clientX;
                const deltaX = clientX - panoStartX;
                
                // Convert pixel movement to percentage movement relative to container width
                const containerWidth = panoContainer.offsetWidth;
                const percentageDelta = (deltaX / containerWidth) * 100;
                
                let newTranslate = currentTranslateX + percentageDelta;
                
                // Clamp
                if(newTranslate > maxTranslate) newTranslate = maxTranslate;
                if(newTranslate < minTranslate) newTranslate = minTranslate;
                
                panoImage.style.transform = `translateX(${newTranslate}%)`;
            }

            window.addEventListener('mouseup', pDragEnd);
            window.addEventListener('touchend', pDragEnd);

            function pDragEnd(e) {
                if(!isPanoDragging) return;
                isPanoDragging = false;
                panoImage.style.transition = 'transform 0.3s ease-out';
                
                // Extract the current transform value
                const style = window.getComputedStyle(panoImage);
                const matrix = new WebKitCSSMatrix(style.transform);
                // Convert matrix tx back to percentage
                currentTranslateX = (matrix.m41 / panoImage.offsetWidth) * 100 * 2; // *2 because image is 200%
            }

            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // DD. Atmospheric AI Simulation Loop
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            setInterval(() => {
                // Simulate slight weather shifts
                const tempEl = document.getElementById('at-temp');
                const windEl = document.getElementById('at-wind');
                
                let temp = parseFloat(tempEl.innerText);
                let wind = parseFloat(windEl.innerText);
                
                temp += (Math.random() * 0.4 - 0.2); // Fluctuate +/- 0.2
                wind += (Math.random() * 2 - 1);
                
                if(wind < 0) wind = 0;
                if(wind > 20) wind = 20;
                
                tempEl.innerText = temp.toFixed(1);
                windEl.innerText = wind.toFixed(1);
            }, 5000);
        </script>
        <style>

                background: var(--bg-surface-1);

                padding: 30px 20px;
                box-shadow: var(--shadow-md);
                position: relative;
                overflow: hidden;
            }
            .vibe-matcher-wrapper::before {
                content: ''; position: absolute; inset: 0;
                background: radial-gradient(circle at top right, var(--gold-muted), transparent 70%);
                pointer-events: none;
                transition: background 0.8s ease;
                id: vibe-bg-glow;
            }

            .vibe-grid {

        <script>
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // EE. Vibe Matcher Logic (CSS Custom Property Overrides)
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            const root = document.documentElement;
            // Store original colors to revert if needed
            const originalGold = getComputedStyle(root).getPropertyValue('--gold-primary').trim();
            const originalShine = getComputedStyle(root).getPropertyValue('--gold-shine').trim();

            const vibeData = {
                royal: { 
                    color: '#D4AF37', shine: '#FFDF00', 
                    title: "The Maharaja Setup", 
                    desc: "A luxurious experience featuring imported velvet pandals, massive crystal chandeliers, and classical warm-white stage lighting perfect for grand weddings."
                },
                neon: { 
                    color: '#b829ff', shine: '#ff00ff', 
                    title: "The Cyber-Club Vibe", 
                    desc: "High-octane atmosphere with 3D RGB lasers, heavy smoke machines, and a towering line-array DJ rig designed for ultimate dance parties."
                },
                bass: { 
                    color: '#ff3333', shine: '#ff6666', 
                    title: "The Earth-Shaker Baraat", 
                    desc: "Pure acoustic violence. Four 21-inch dual subwoofers mounted on a moving trolley, firing devastating bass drops for the ultimate street procession."
                },
                corp: { 
                    color: '#00e5ff', shine: '#00ffff', 
                    title: "The Executive Gala", 
                    desc: "Sleek, professional, and immaculate. Crisp PA audio, clean architectural uplighting, and flawless silent power delivery for VIP functions."
                }
            };

            function applyVibe(vibeId, element) {
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                
                // Update active classes
                document.querySelectorAll('.vibe-card').forEach(c => c.classList.remove('active'));
                element.classList.add('active');

                // Apply CSS Variable Shifts globally
                root.style.setProperty('--gold-primary', vibeData[vibeId].color);
                root.style.setProperty('--gold-shine', vibeData[vibeId].shine);
                
                // Update Result Box
                const resBox = document.getElementById('vibeResult');
                const title = document.getElementById('vibeResTitle');
                const desc = document.getElementById('vibeResDesc');
                
                resBox.style.display = 'none'; // reset animation
                setTimeout(() => {
                    title.innerText = vibeData[vibeId].title;
                    title.style.color = vibeData[vibeId].color;
                    desc.innerText = vibeData[vibeId].desc;
                    resBox.style.display = 'block';
                    resBox.style.borderColor = vibeData[vibeId].color;
                }, 50);
            }

            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // FF. Smart Capacity Matrix Logic
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            function calculateCapacity(guests) {
                if(typeof playTap === 'function' && guests % 200 === 0) playTap(); // Tick sound occasionally
                
                const gVal = document.getElementById('guestCountVal');
                const sqftVal = document.getElementById('sqftVal');
                const tentRecVal = document.getElementById('tentRecVal');
                const floorplan = document.getElementById('virtualFloorplan');
                
                gVal.innerText = guests;
                
                // Math: 15 sq ft per person (Standard luxury dining + stage buffer)
                const totalSqFt = guests * 15;
                sqftVal.innerText = totalSqFt.toLocaleString();

                // Generate approximate dimensions (assuming standard widths like 40, 60, 80)
                let width, length;
                if (totalSqFt <= 2400) { width = 40; length = Math.ceil(totalSqFt / 40); }
                else if (totalSqFt <= 6000) { width = 60; length = Math.ceil(totalSqFt / 60); }
                else if (totalSqFt <= 10000) { width = 80; length = Math.ceil(totalSqFt / 80); }
                else { width = 100; length = Math.ceil(totalSqFt / 100); }
                
                // Round length up to nearest 10
                length = Math.ceil(length / 10) * 10;
                tentRecVal.innerText = `${width} x ${length} Ft`;

                // Update Virtual Floorplan (Visual Representation)
                // We won't render 2000 dots as it lags mobile. We render scaled ratios.
                floorplan.innerHTML = '<div class="floorplan-overlay"></div>'; // clear existing
                
                const dotCount = Math.min(Math.floor(guests / 10), 100); // 1 dot = 10 guests, max 100 dots
                const tableCount = Math.floor(dotCount / 5);

                // Add tables first
                for(let i=0; i<tableCount; i++) {
                    const table = document.createElement('div');
                    table.className = 'table-dot';
                    table.style.animationDelay = `${Math.random() * 0.2}s`;
                    floorplan.appendChild(table);
                }
                
                // Add guests
                for(let i=0; i<dotCount; i++) {
                    const dot = document.createElement('div');
                    dot.className = 'guest-dot';
                    dot.style.animationDelay = `${Math.random() * 0.3}s`;
                    floorplan.appendChild(dot);
                }
            }
            
            // Init capacity visually
            calculateCapacity(500);

            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // GG. DMX Laser Simulator (Canvas Engine)
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            const dmxCanvas = document.getElementById('dmxCanvas');
            const dctx = dmxCanvas.getContext('2d', { alpha: false }); // Optimize for no transparency bg
            let laserW, laserH;
            
            // Track multiple touches/mouse
            const activeBeams = [];

            function resizeDmxCanvas() {
                const rect = dmxCanvas.parentElement.getBoundingClientRect();
                dmxCanvas.width = rect.width;
                dmxCanvas.height = rect.height;
                laserW = dmxCanvas.width;
                laserH = dmxCanvas.height;
                dctx.fillStyle = '#000';
                dctx.fillRect(0, 0, laserW, laserH);
            }
            window.addEventListener('resize', resizeDmxCanvas);
            resizeDmxCanvas();

            // Light Source Points (Mapping to the HTML rig bulbs)
            function getLightSources() {
                return [
                    {x: laserW * 0.1, y: laserH},
                    {x: laserW * 0.3, y: laserH},
                    {x: laserW * 0.5, y: laserH},
                    {x: laserW * 0.7, y: laserH},
                    {x: laserW * 0.9, y: laserH}
                ];
            }

            function drawLasers() {
                // Fade out old frames (Motion Blur)
                dctx.globalCompositeOperation = 'source-over';
                dctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.2)'; // Alpha controls tail length
                dctx.fillRect(0, 0, laserW, laserH);

                dctx.globalCompositeOperation = 'lighter'; // Additive blending for light
                const sources = getLightSources();
                const colors = ['#ff3333', '#00ff00', '#00e5ff', '#ff00ff', '#FFD700'];

                activeBeams.forEach((target) => {
                    sources.forEach((src, idx) => {
                        // Draw volumetric beam
                        dctx.beginPath();
                        dctx.moveTo(src.x, src.y);
                        
                        // Add slight spread/scatter at the target for realism
                        const spreadX = target.x + (Math.random() * 10 - 5);
                        const spreadY = target.y + (Math.random() * 10 - 5);
                        
                        dctx.lineTo(spreadX, spreadY);
                        dctx.lineWidth = Math.random() * 3 + 1; // Flickering width
                        dctx.strokeStyle = colors[idx % colors.length];
                        
                        // Create gradient for beam fade
                        const grad = dctx.createLinearGradient(src.x, src.y, target.x, target.y);
                        grad.addColorStop(0, colors[idx % colors.length]);
                        grad.addColorStop(1, 'transparent');
                        dctx.strokeStyle = grad;
                        
                        dctx.stroke();

                        // Flash corresponding HTML bulb
                        const bulb = document.getElementById(`bulb${idx+1}`);
                        if(bulb) {
                            bulb.style.background = colors[idx % colors.length];
                            bulb.style.boxShadow = `0 -5px 15px ${colors[idx % colors.length]}`;
                        }
                    });
                });

                // Reset bulbs if no beams
                if(activeBeams.length === 0) {
                    for(let i=1; i<=5; i++) {
                        const bulb = document.getElementById(`bulb${i}`);
                        if(bulb) { bulb.style.background = '#333'; bulb.style.boxShadow = 'none'; }
                    }
                }

                requestAnimationFrame(drawLasers);
            }
            drawLasers(); // Start loop

            // Input Handlers
            function updateBeams(e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                activeBeams.length = 0; // Clear array
                
                if(e.type.includes('touch')) {
                    for(let i=0; i<e.touches.length; i++) {
                        const rect = dmxCanvas.getBoundingClientRect();
                        activeBeams.push({
                            x: e.touches[i].clientX - rect.left,
                            y: e.touches[i].clientY - rect.top
                        });
                    }
                } else {
                    const rect = dmxCanvas.getBoundingClientRect();
                    activeBeams.push({
                        x: e.clientX - rect.left,
                        y: e.clientY - rect.top
                    });
                }
            }

            function clearBeams() { activeBeams.length = 0; }

            dmxCanvas.addEventListener('mousedown', (e) => { updateBeams(e); dmxCanvas.addEventListener('mousemove', updateBeams); });
            window.addEventListener('mouseup', () => { clearBeams(); dmxCanvas.removeEventListener('mousemove', updateBeams); });
            
            dmxCanvas.addEventListener('touchstart', updateBeams, {passive: false});
            dmxCanvas.addEventListener('touchmove', updateBeams, {passive: false});
            dmxCanvas.addEventListener('touchend', clearBeams);
            dmxCanvas.addEventListener('touchcancel', clearBeams);
        </script>
        <style>

        <script>
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // HH. AR Vision Engine (Camera & Wireframe Canvas)
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            let arStream = null;
            const arVideo = document.getElementById('arVideoFeed');
            const arHud = document.getElementById('arHud');
            const arInitOverlay = document.getElementById('arInitOverlay');
            const arControls = document.getElementById('arControls');
            const arCanvas = document.getElementById('arWireframeCanvas');
            let arCtx = null;
            let arAnimFrame = null;
            let currentArModel = 'dj'; // 'dj' or 'tent'
            let pitchVal = 0;

            async function initArCamera() {
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                arInitOverlay.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-satellite-dish fa-spin" style="font-size:40px; color:#00e5ff; margin-bottom:20px;"></i><h3 style="color:#00e5ff; font-family:Orbitron;">ESTABLISHING UPLINK...</h3>';
                
                try {
                    // Request rear camera
                    arStream = await navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia({ 
                        video: { facingMode: 'environment' } 
                    });
                    
                    arVideo.srcObject = arStream;
                    
                    arVideo.onloadedmetadata = () => {
                        arVideo.style.opacity = '1';
                        arInitOverlay.style.display = 'none';
                        arHud.style.display = 'block';
                        arControls.style.display = 'flex';
                        
                        // Setup Canvas Overlay
                        arCanvas.width = arVideo.clientWidth;
                        arCanvas.height = arVideo.clientHeight;
                        arCtx = arCanvas.getContext('2d');
                        
                        // Start Device Orientation tracking if available (for Pitch)
                        if (window.DeviceOrientationEvent) {
                            window.addEventListener('deviceorientation', handleOrientation);
                        }
                        
                        drawArWireframe();
                        showToast("AR Vision Active. Scan Venue.");
                    };
                } catch(err) {
                    console.error("AR Error:", err);
                    arInitOverlay.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-exclamation-triangle" style="font-size:40px; color:#ff3333; margin-bottom:20px;"></i><h3 style="color:#ff3333; font-family:Orbitron;">HARDWARE LOCKOUT</h3><p style="font-size:12px; color:#aaa;">Camera access denied or unsupported. Switch to manual mode.</p>';
                    setTimeout(() => { arInitOverlay.style.display = 'flex'; }, 2000);
                }
            }

            function stopArCamera() {
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                if(arStream) {
                    arStream.getTracks().forEach(track => track.stop());
                    arStream = null;
                }
                arVideo.style.opacity = '0';
                arHud.style.display = 'none';
                arControls.style.display = 'none';
                arInitOverlay.style.display = 'flex';
                arInitOverlay.innerHTML = `
                    <i class="fas fa-camera" style="font-size: 50px; color: var(--gold-primary); margin-bottom: 20px;"></i>
                    <h3 style="color: #fff; font-family: 'Cinzel'; font-size: 20px; margin-bottom: 10px;">ENVIRONMENT SCANNER</h3>
                    <button class="f-btn" style="max-width: 250px; background: linear-gradient(90deg, #00e5ff, #0088cc); color: #000; margin-top:20px;" onclick="initArCamera()"><i class="fas fa-power-off"></i> RE-INITIALIZE</button>
                `;
                if(arAnimFrame) cancelAnimationFrame(arAnimFrame);
                if(arCtx) arCtx.clearRect(0, 0, arCanvas.width, arCanvas.height);
                window.removeEventListener('deviceorientation', handleOrientation);
            }

            function switchArModel(model) {
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                currentArModel = model;
                document.getElementById('arStatusTxt').innerText = `REC // RENDER: MND ${model.toUpperCase()} MATRIX`;
                if(navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate(20);
            }

            function handleOrientation(e) {
                // Alpha, Beta, Gamma
                pitchVal = Math.round(e.beta || 0);
                const pitchText = document.getElementById('arPitch');
                if(pitchText) pitchText.innerText = pitchVal;
            }

            // Draw spinning 3D-ish wireframes on Canvas over the video
            let arRotation = 0;
            function drawArWireframe() {
                if(!arStream) return;
                arAnimFrame = requestAnimationFrame(drawArWireframe);
                
                arCtx.clearRect(0, 0, arCanvas.width, arCanvas.height);
                
                const cx = arCanvas.width / 2;
                // Move Y based on pitch to simulate stabilization
                const cy = (arCanvas.height / 2) + (pitchVal * 2); 
                
                arCtx.save();
                arCtx.translate(cx, cy);
                arCtx.rotate(arRotation);
                
                arCtx.lineWidth = 2;
                
                if(currentArModel === 'dj') {
                    // Draw DJ Speaker Stack Wireframe
                    arCtx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(0, 229, 255, 0.8)';
                    arCtx.strokeRect(-40, -60, 80, 120);
                    arCtx.beginPath();
                    arCtx.arc(0, 20, 25, 0, Math.PI * 2); // Sub
                    arCtx.stroke();
                    arCtx.beginPath();
                    arCtx.arc(0, -30, 15, 0, Math.PI * 2); // Top
                    arCtx.stroke();
                } else if (currentArModel === 'tent') {
                    // Draw Tent/Truss Wireframe
                    arCtx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(212, 175, 55, 0.8)';
                    arCtx.beginPath();
                    arCtx.moveTo(-80, 50);
                    arCtx.lineTo(80, 50); // Floor
                    arCtx.lineTo(80, -30); // Right Wall
                    arCtx.lineTo(0, -80); // Roof Peak
                    arCtx.lineTo(-80, -30); // Left Wall
                    arCtx.closePath();
                    arCtx.stroke();
                    // Truss cross lines
                    arCtx.beginPath();
                    arCtx.moveTo(-80, 50); arCtx.lineTo(80, -30);
                    arCtx.moveTo(80, 50); arCtx.lineTo(-80, -30);
                    arCtx.stroke();
                }
                
                arCtx.restore();
                arRotation += 0.02; // Spin speed
            }

            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // II. Acoustic Topography Heatmap Logic
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            const topoCanvas = document.getElementById('topoCanvas');
            const topoWrap = document.getElementById('topoWrap');
            let tCtx = null;
            let subs = []; // Array of placed subwoofers
            let topoAnim = null;
            let wavePhase = 0;

            function initTopo() {
                topoCanvas.width = topoWrap.clientWidth;
                topoCanvas.height = topoWrap.clientHeight;
                tCtx = topoCanvas.getContext('2d');
            }
            window.addEventListener('resize', initTopo);
            initTopo();

            // Click to add a subwoofer source
            topoCanvas.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                const rect = topoCanvas.getBoundingClientRect();
                const x = e.clientX - rect.left;
                const y = e.clientY - rect.top;
                
                subs.push({x, y, power: Math.random() * 50 + 100}); // Radius power
                if(navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate(30);
                
                if(!topoAnim) animateTopo();
            });

            function clearTopo() {
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                subs = [];
                tCtx.clearRect(0, 0, topoCanvas.width, topoCanvas.height);
                if(topoAnim) { cancelAnimationFrame(topoAnim); topoAnim = null; }
            }

            function simulateDrop() {
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                // Temporarily boost power of all subs to max
                subs.forEach(s => s.power = 250);
                // Shake the canvas container
                topoWrap.style.animation = 'heavyBassShake 0.5s';
                if(navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate([100, 50, 200, 50, 400]);
                setTimeout(() => {
                    topoWrap.style.animation = '';
                    subs.forEach(s => s.power = Math.random() * 50 + 100); // Return to normal
                }, 500);
                
                if(!topoAnim && subs.length > 0) animateTopo();
            }

            function animateTopo() {
                if(subs.length === 0) return;
                topoAnim = requestAnimationFrame(animateTopo);
                
                // Clear with deep black for blending
                tCtx.fillStyle = '#000';
                tCtx.fillRect(0, 0, topoCanvas.width, topoCanvas.height);
                
                // Additive blending makes overlapping sounds "hotter" (white/yellow)
                tCtx.globalCompositeOperation = 'lighter';
                
                wavePhase += 0.1; // Pulse speed

                subs.forEach(sub => {
                    // Pulsing radius
                    const currentRadius = sub.power + (Math.sin(wavePhase) * 10);
                    
                    if(currentRadius > 0) {
                        const gradient = tCtx.createRadialGradient(sub.x, sub.y, 0, sub.x, sub.y, currentRadius);
                        
                        // Thermal Color Mapping (Center is hot, edges are cool)
                        gradient.addColorStop(0, 'rgba(255, 0, 0, 1)');      // Center: Red/White hot
                        gradient.addColorStop(0.3, 'rgba(255, 255, 0, 0.8)');// Mid: Yellow
                        gradient.addColorStop(0.6, 'rgba(0, 255, 0, 0.5)');  // Far: Green
                        gradient.addColorStop(1, 'rgba(0, 0, 255, 0)');      // Edge: Blue fading out
                        
                        tCtx.fillStyle = gradient;
                        tCtx.beginPath();
                        tCtx.arc(sub.x, sub.y, currentRadius, 0, Math.PI * 2);
                        tCtx.fill();
                        
                        // Draw the physical sub box in the center
                        tCtx.globalCompositeOperation = 'source-over';
                        tCtx.fillStyle = '#fff';
                        tCtx.fillRect(sub.x - 4, sub.y - 4, 8, 8);
                        tCtx.globalCompositeOperation = 'lighter';
                    }
                });
                tCtx.globalCompositeOperation = 'source-over'; // Reset for next frame
            }

            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // JJ. Royal Protocol Timeline Logic (UI & Audio Sync)
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            function activateProtocol(nodeElement, phase) {
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                
                // Update active UI classes
                document.querySelectorAll('.timeline-node').forEach(n => n.classList.remove('active'));
                nodeElement.classList.add('active');
                
                // Smooth scroll track to center the clicked node
                const track = document.getElementById('eventProtocolTrack');
                const scrollPos = nodeElement.offsetLeft - (track.offsetWidth / 2) + (nodeElement.offsetWidth / 2);
                track.scrollTo({ left: scrollPos, behavior: 'smooth' });

                // Vibe & Audio logic based on phase
                if(engineOn && proCtx) {
                    const t = proCtx.currentTime;
                    switch(phase) {
                        case 'baraat':
                            // Heavy Bass hit
                            const bOsc = proCtx.createOscillator();
                            const bGain = proCtx.createGain();
                            bOsc.type = 'triangle'; bOsc.frequency.setValueAtTime(60, t);
                            bOsc.frequency.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(20, t + 1);
                            bOsc.connect(bGain); bGain.connect(subBassGain);
                            bGain.gain.setValueAtTime(1, t); bGain.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.01, t + 1);
                            bOsc.start(t); bOsc.stop(t + 1);
                            document.body.style.boxShadow = 'inset 0 0 50px rgba(212,175,55,0.2)';
                            break;
                            
                        case 'varmala':
                            // Angelic Synth Sweep
                            const vOsc = proCtx.createOscillator();
                            const vGain = proCtx.createGain();
                            vOsc.type = 'sine'; vOsc.frequency.setValueAtTime(800, t);
                            vOsc.frequency.linearRampToValueAtTime(1200, t + 2);
                            vOsc.connect(vGain); vGain.connect(masterVol);
                            vGain.gain.setValueAtTime(0, t); vGain.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0.5, t + 1); vGain.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0, t + 2);
                            vOsc.start(t); vOsc.stop(t + 2);
                            document.body.style.boxShadow = 'inset 0 0 50px rgba(184,41,255,0.2)';
                            break;
                            
                        case 'phera':
                            // Deep Bell toll
                            const pOsc = proCtx.createOscillator();
                            const pGain = proCtx.createGain();
                            pOsc.type = 'sine'; pOsc.frequency.setValueAtTime(300, t);
                            pOsc.connect(pGain); pGain.connect(masterVol);
                            pGain.gain.setValueAtTime(0.8, t); pGain.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.01, t + 3);
                            pOsc.start(t); pOsc.stop(t + 3);
                            document.body.style.boxShadow = 'inset 0 0 50px rgba(255,51,51,0.2)';
                            break;
                            
                        case 'reception':
                            // Club Laser Pluck
                            const rOsc = proCtx.createOscillator();
                            const rGain = proCtx.createGain();
                            rOsc.type = 'sawtooth'; rOsc.frequency.setValueAtTime(2000, t);
                            rOsc.frequency.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(100, t + 0.3);
                            rOsc.connect(rGain); rGain.connect(distNode);
                            rGain.gain.setValueAtTime(0.6, t); rGain.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.01, t + 0.3);
                            rOsc.start(t); rOsc.stop(t + 0.3);
                            document.body.style.boxShadow = 'inset 0 0 50px rgba(0,229,255,0.2)';
                            break;
                    }
                } else {
                    // Visual fallback if audio engine is off
                    showToast(`Activating ${phase.toUpperCase()} visual protocol...`);
                }
            }
        </script>

                <div class="inv-row"><span>Logistics Surcharge</span><span id="invLogCost">₹0</span></div>
                <div class="inv-row" style="color:#888; font-size:12px;"><span>Tax (GST)</span><span>Included</span></div>
                
                <div class="inv-row inv-total"><span>ESTIMATED TOTAL</span><span id="invTotalCost">₹0</span></div>

                <div class="signature-box">
                    <span class="sig-label">CLIENT E-SIGNATURE:</span>
                    <canvas id="sigCanvas"></canvas>
                    <div class="sig-line"></div>
                </div>

                <div style="display:flex; justify-content:space-between; margin-top:15px;">
                    <button style="background:transparent; border:none; color:#ff3333; font-weight:bold; cursor:pointer;" onclick="clearSignature()"><i class="fas fa-eraser"></i> Clear</button>
                    <button class="f-btn" style="width: auto; padding: 10px 20px; border-radius: 5px; font-size: 12px; color:#fff;" onclick="showToast('Contract Locked & Encrypted!')"><i class="fas fa-lock"></i> AUTHORIZE</button>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>

        <script>
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // KK. Auto-Mixer Physics & Interaction (Dual Decks)
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            let deckAOn = false;
            let deckBOn = false;
            let vuIntervalA, vuIntervalB;

            function toggleDeck(deck) {
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                const record = document.getElementById(`record${deck}`);
                const deckContainer = document.getElementById(`deck${deck}`);
                
                if(deck === 'A') {
                    deckAOn = !deckAOn;
                    if(deckAOn) {
                        record.classList.add('spinning');
                        deckContainer.classList.add('active');
                        vuIntervalA = setInterval(() => animateVU(`vuA`), 150);
                    } else {
                        record.classList.remove('spinning');
                        deckContainer.classList.remove('active');
                        clearInterval(vuIntervalA);
                        resetVU(`vuA`);
                    }
                } else {
                    deckBOn = !deckBOn;
                    if(deckBOn) {
                        record.classList.add('spinning');
                        deckContainer.classList.add('active');
                        vuIntervalB = setInterval(() => animateVU(`vuB`), 150);
                    } else {
                        record.classList.remove('spinning');
                        deckContainer.classList.remove('active');
                        clearInterval(vuIntervalB);
                        resetVU(`vuB`);
                    }
                }
            }

            function animateVU(meterId) {
                const leds = document.getElementById(meterId).querySelectorAll('.vu-led');
                // Random intensity 0 to 6
                const intensity = Math.floor(Math.random() * 7);
                
                leds.forEach((led, idx) => {
                    led.className = 'vu-led'; // reset
                    if(idx < intensity) {
                        if(idx < 3) led.classList.add('active-g');
                        else if(idx < 5) led.classList.add('active-y');
                        else led.classList.add('active-r');
                    }
                });
            }

            function resetVU(meterId) {
                const leds = document.getElementById(meterId).querySelectorAll('.vu-led');
                leds.forEach(led => led.className = 'vu-led');
            }

            // Scratching Physics
            let isScratching = false;
            let scratchStartX = 0;
            let targetRecord = null;

            function startScratch(deck, e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                isScratching = true;
                targetRecord = document.getElementById(`record${deck}`);
                scratchStartX = e.type.includes('touch') ? e.touches[0].clientX : e.clientX;
                
                // Pause animation during scratch
                targetRecord.style.animationPlayState = 'paused';
                if(engineOn) enginePlay('snare1', targetRecord); // Synthesize a scratch sound
            }

            function performScratch(e) {
                if(!isScratching || !targetRecord) return;
                const currentX = e.type.includes('touch') ? e.touches[0].clientX : e.clientX;
                const deltaX = currentX - scratchStartX;
                
                // Apply manual rotation
                targetRecord.style.transform = `rotate(${deltaX * 2}deg)`;
                
                // Continuous sound triggering for realistic feel
                if(Math.abs(deltaX) % 30 < 5 && engineOn) {
                    enginePlay('hihatC', targetRecord);
                }
            }

            function endScratch() {
                if(!isScratching) return;
                isScratching = false;
                if(targetRecord) {
                    targetRecord.style.transform = '';
                    targetRecord.style.animationPlayState = 'running';
                    targetRecord = null;
                }
            }

            window.addEventListener('mousemove', performScratch);
            window.addEventListener('touchmove', performScratch, {passive:false});
            window.addEventListener('mouseup', endScratch);
            window.addEventListener('touchend', endScratch);

            // Crossfader Logic
            const cfTrack = document.getElementById('cfTrack');
            const cfKnob = document.getElementById('cfKnob');
            let isFading = false;

            cfKnob.addEventListener('mousedown', (e) => { isFading = true; e.preventDefault(); });
            cfKnob.addEventListener('touchstart', (e) => { isFading = true; }, {passive:true});

            window.addEventListener('mousemove', (e) => {
                if(!isFading) return;
                const rect = cfTrack.getBoundingClientRect();
                let x = e.clientX - rect.left;
                if(x < 0) x = 0;
                if(x > rect.width) x = rect.width;
                cfKnob.style.left = `${x}px`;
            });
            window.addEventListener('touchmove', (e) => {
                if(!isFading) return;
                const rect = cfTrack.getBoundingClientRect();
                let x = e.touches[0].clientX - rect.left;
                if(x < 0) x = 0;
                if(x > rect.width) x = rect.width;
                cfKnob.style.left = `${x}px`;
            }, {passive:true});

            window.addEventListener('mouseup', () => isFading = false);
            window.addEventListener('touchend', () => isFading = false);

            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // LL. Drone Mapper Logic
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            const droneCanvas = document.getElementById('droneCanvas');
            const dcCtx = droneCanvas.getContext('2d');
            const vDrone = document.getElementById('vDrone');
            const waypoints = [];

            function resizeDroneCanvas() {
                const rect = droneCanvas.parentElement.getBoundingClientRect();
                droneCanvas.width = rect.width;
                droneCanvas.height = rect.height;
            }
            window.addEventListener('resize', resizeDroneCanvas);
            resizeDroneCanvas();

            droneCanvas.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                const rect = droneCanvas.getBoundingClientRect();
                const x = e.clientX - rect.left;
                const y = e.clientY - rect.top;
                
                waypoints.push({x, y});
                document.getElementById('droneWpCount').innerText = waypoints.length;
                document.getElementById('droneSweepTime').innerText = `00:${(waypoints.length * 12).toString().padStart(2, '0')}`;
                
                drawDronePath();
                moveDroneTo(x, y);
            });

            function drawDronePath() {
                dcCtx.clearRect(0, 0, droneCanvas.width, droneCanvas.height);
                if(waypoints.length === 0) return;

                // Draw Path
                dcCtx.beginPath();
                dcCtx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(0, 255, 0, 0.5)';
                dcCtx.lineWidth = 2;
                dcCtx.setLineDash([5, 5]);
                dcCtx.moveTo(waypoints[0].x, waypoints[0].y);
                for(let i=1; i<waypoints.length; i++) {
                    dcCtx.lineTo(waypoints[i].x, waypoints[i].y);
                }
                dcCtx.stroke();

                // Draw Nodes
                dcCtx.setLineDash([]);
                waypoints.forEach((wp, index) => {
                    dcCtx.beginPath();
                    dcCtx.fillStyle = '#000';
                    dcCtx.strokeStyle = '#00ff00';
                    dcCtx.arc(wp.x, wp.y, 6, 0, Math.PI * 2);
                    dcCtx.fill();
                    dcCtx.stroke();
                    
                    dcCtx.fillStyle = '#00ff00';
                    dcCtx.font = '10px Orbitron';
                    dcCtx.fillText(index+1, wp.x - 3, wp.y + 3);
                });
            }

            function moveDroneTo(x, y) {
                vDrone.style.left = `${x}px`;
                vDrone.style.top = `${y}px`;
            }

            function clearDronePath() {
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                waypoints.length = 0;
                dcCtx.clearRect(0, 0, droneCanvas.width, droneCanvas.height);
                document.getElementById('droneWpCount').innerText = '0';
                document.getElementById('droneSweepTime').innerText = '00:00';
                // Reset to center
                vDrone.style.left = '50%';
                vDrone.style.top = '50%';
            }

            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // MM. E-Signature Invoice Generator Logic
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            const sigCanvas = document.getElementById('sigCanvas');
            const sigCtx = sigCanvas.getContext('2d');
            let isSigning = false;

            function initSignature() {
                // Adjust for high DPI to prevent blurry lines
                const rect = sigCanvas.getBoundingClientRect();
                sigCanvas.width = rect.width;
                sigCanvas.height = rect.height;
                sigCtx.lineWidth = 2;
                sigCtx.strokeStyle = '#000088'; // Blue ink pen color
                sigCtx.lineCap = 'round';
                sigCtx.lineJoin = 'round';
            }
            window.addEventListener('resize', initSignature);
            initSignature();

            function getSigPos(e) {
                const rect = sigCanvas.getBoundingClientRect();
                const clientX = e.type.includes('touch') ? e.touches[0].clientX : e.clientX;
                const clientY = e.type.includes('touch') ? e.touches[0].clientY : e.clientY;
                return { x: clientX - rect.left, y: clientY - rect.top };
            }

            function startSig(e) {
                isSigning = true;
                const pos = getSigPos(e);
                sigCtx.beginPath();
                sigCtx.moveTo(pos.x, pos.y);
                e.preventDefault(); // Prevent scrolling on mobile
            }

            function drawSig(e) {
                if(!isSigning) return;
                const pos = getSigPos(e);
                sigCtx.lineTo(pos.x, pos.y);
                sigCtx.stroke();
                e.preventDefault();
            }

            function endSig() {
                isSigning = false;
            }

            sigCanvas.addEventListener('mousedown', startSig);
            sigCanvas.addEventListener('mousemove', drawSig);
            window.addEventListener('mouseup', endSig);

            sigCanvas.addEventListener('touchstart', startSig, {passive: false});
            sigCanvas.addEventListener('touchmove', drawSig, {passive: false});
            window.addEventListener('touchend', endSig);

            function clearSignature() {
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                sigCtx.clearRect(0, 0, sigCanvas.width, sigCanvas.height);
            }

            // Sync Smart Quote to Invoice
            // Overriding the previous animateQuoteValue to also update invoice
            if (typeof window.animateQuoteValue === 'function') {
                const oldAnimate = window.animateQuoteValue;
                window.animateQuoteValue = function(finalVal) {
                    oldAnimate(finalVal); // Call original
                    
                    // Update Invoice
                    const baseCostEl = document.getElementById('invBaseCost');
                    const totalCostEl = document.getElementById('invTotalCost');
                    const logCostEl = document.getElementById('invLogCost');
                    
                    if(baseCostEl && totalCostEl) {
                        baseCostEl.innerText = `₹${finalVal.toLocaleString()}`;
                        
                        // Parse logistics cost safely
                        let logCostStr = logCostEl.innerText.replace('₹', '').replace(/,/g, '');
                        let logCost = parseInt(logCostStr) || 0;
                        
                        const total = finalVal + logCost;
                        totalCostEl.innerText = `₹${total.toLocaleString()}`;
                    }
                };
            }
        </script>

        <style>

                position: relative;
                perspective: 1000px; /* Crucial for 3D flip */
            }

            .vip-inputs {
                display: flex; flex-direction: column; gap: 15px; margin-bottom: 30px;
            }

            .vip-card-3d {
                width: 100%;
                max-width: 320px;
                height: 500px;

                transform-style: preserve-3d;
                transition: transform 0.8s cubic-bezier(0.175, 0.885, 0.32, 1.275);

        <style>
            .sub-sim-wrapper {
                background: #0a0a0f;
                border: 2px solid #222;
                border-radius: var(--border-radius-lg);
                margin-top: 60px;
                padding: 40px 20px;
                text-align: center;
                box-shadow: inset 0 0 50px rgba(0,0,0,0.9);
            }

            .speaker-cabinet {
                width: 250px;
                height: 250px;
                margin: 0 auto 30px auto;
                background: linear-gradient(145deg, #1a1a1a, #0d0d0d);
                border: 4px solid #333;
                border-radius: 20px;
                display: flex;
                justify-content: center;
                align-items: center;
                position: relative;
                box-shadow: 0 20px 40px rgba(0,0,0,0.8), inset 0 0 10px rgba(255,255,255,0.05);
            }
            
            /* Cabinet Screws */

        <div class="showcase-container reveal-on-scroll">
            <h2 class="section-label-pro"><i class="fas fa-wave-square"></i> ACOUSTIC EXCURSION SIMULATOR</h2>
