        <script>
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // NN. Master Settings Logic
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            let globalHaptic = true;
            let batterySaver = false;

            function toggleSetting(setting, el) {
                if(globalHaptic && navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate(15);
                el.classList.toggle('active');
                const isActive = el.classList.contains('active');

                if(setting === 'eye') {
                    if(isActive) document.body.classList.add('eye-comfort');
                    else document.body.classList.remove('eye-comfort');
                    // Mutual exclusion with contrast
                    if(isActive && document.getElementById('togContrast').classList.contains('active')) {
                        toggleSetting('contrast', document.getElementById('togContrast'));
                    }
                } 
                else if(setting === 'contrast') {
                    if(isActive) document.body.classList.add('high-contrast');
                    else document.body.classList.remove('high-contrast');
                    if(isActive && document.getElementById('togEye').classList.contains('active')) {
                        toggleSetting('eye', document.getElementById('togEye'));
                    }
                }
                else if(setting === 'haptic') {
                    globalHaptic = isActive;
                }
                else if(setting === 'battery') {
                    batterySaver = isActive;
                    if(batterySaver) {
                        // Pause heavy canvas operations
                        if(window.animFrame) cancelAnimationFrame(window.animFrame);
                        if(window.topoAnim) cancelAnimationFrame(window.topoAnim);
                        clearEffectLayer(); // From part 10
                        showToast("Battery Saver: Background Renders Paused");
                    } else {
                        showToast("Battery Saver: Max Performance Restored");
                    }
                }
            }

            function changeSystemFont(fontVal) {
                document.body.style.fontFamily = fontVal;
                showToast("System Typography Updated");
            }

            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // OO. VIP Pass Generator Logic
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            function updateVIPCard() {
                const nameIn = document.getElementById('vipEventInput').value.trim();
                const dateIn = document.getElementById('vipDateInput').value;
                
                const nameDisplay = document.getElementById('vipCardName');
                const dateDisplay = document.getElementById('vipCardDate');
                const serialDisplay = document.getElementById('vipSerial');

                nameDisplay.innerText = nameIn ? nameIn : "YOUR EVENT NAME";
                
                if(dateIn) {
                    const d = new Date(dateIn);
                    dateDisplay.innerText = d.toLocaleDateString('en-IN', { day:'2-digit', month:'short', year:'numeric'}).toUpperCase();
                    
                    // Generate a fake hash serial based on date/name
                    const hash = btoa(nameIn + dateIn).substring(0, 8).toUpperCase();
                    serialDisplay.innerText = `MND-${hash}`;
                } else {
                    dateDisplay.innerText = "SELECT DATE";
                    serialDisplay.innerText = "MND-00000000";
                }
            }

            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // PP. Subwoofer Physics Excursion Simulator Logic
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            const cone = document.getElementById('speakerCone');
            const hzDisplay = document.getElementById('hzVal');
            let hzInterval = null;
            let isTestingBass = false;
            let currentHz = 40;
            let testOsc = null;
            let testGain = null;

            function updateHz(val) {
                currentHz = parseInt(val);
                hzDisplay.innerText = currentHz;
                
                // If audio is playing, update frequency live
                if(isTestingBass && testOsc) {
                    testOsc.frequency.setValueAtTime(currentHz, proCtx.currentTime);
                }
            }

            function animateCone() {
                if(!isTestingBass) return;

                // The physics logic: Lower Hz = Slower but LARGER excursion (movement).
                // Higher Hz = Faster but SMALLER excursion.
                
                // Calculate excursion amplitude (scale)
                // At 10Hz, scale is massive (1.3). At 100Hz, scale is tiny (1.05).
                const maxScale = 1.0 + (30 / currentHz); 
                const minScale = 1.0 - (10 / currentHz);
                
                // Use a sine wave based on time and Hz to animate
                const time = Date.now() / 1000; // seconds
                // Math.sin needs radians. 1 Hz = 2 * PI radians per second.
                const wave = Math.sin(time * currentHz * Math.PI * 2);
                
                // Map wave (-1 to 1) to scale
                const scale = wave > 0 
                    ? 1.0 + (wave * (maxScale - 1.0)) 
                    : 1.0 + (wave * (1.0 - minScale));

                cone.style.transform = `scale(${scale})`;

                // Throttle animation frame based on battery saver
                if(!batterySaver) {
                    requestAnimationFrame(animateCone);
                } else {
                    setTimeout(() => requestAnimationFrame(animateCone), 30);
                }
            }

            function toggleBassTest() {
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                const btn = document.getElementById('btnTestBass');
                
                if(!isTestingBass) {
                    isTestingBass = true;
                    btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-stop"></i> STOP TEST';
                    btn.style.background = '#222';
                    btn.style.border = '1px solid var(--accent-red)';
                    
                    // Audio Engine Integration
                    if(engineOn && proCtx) {
                        testOsc = proCtx.createOscillator();
                        testGain = proCtx.createGain();
                        testOsc.type = 'sine';
                        testOsc.frequency.value = currentHz;
                        
                        testOsc.connect(testGain);
                        testGain.connect(subBassGain); // Route to deep bass channel defined in Part 13/14
                        
                        // Soft attack
                        testGain.gain.setValueAtTime(0, proCtx.currentTime);
                        testGain.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(2.0, proCtx.currentTime + 0.5);
                        
                        testOsc.start();
                    } else {
                        showToast("Visual physics mode only. Turn on Audio Engine in Studio for sound.");
                    }
                    
                    animateCone();
                    
                } else {
                    isTestingBass = false;
                    btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-play"></i> INITIATE FREQUENCY TEST';
                    btn.style.background = 'var(--accent-red)';
                    btn.style.border = 'none';
                    cone.style.transform = 'scale(1)'; // Reset
                    
                    if(testOsc && testGain) {
                        testGain.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0, proCtx.currentTime + 0.5);
                        testOsc.stop(proCtx.currentTime + 0.5);
                        testOsc = null;
                    }
                }
            }
        </script>

            }
            .comm-btn:hover {
                background: #00e5ff; color: #000; box-shadow: 0 0 20px #00e5ff;
            }
        </style>

        <div class="showcase-container reveal-on-scroll">
            <h2 class="section-label-pro"><i class="fas fa-satellite-dish"></i> SECURE COMM-LINK</h2>
            
            <div class="comm-link-wrapper">
                <div class="comm-terminal">
                    <div class="comm-header">
                        <h3 class="comm-title"><i class="fas fa-shield-alt"></i> ENCRYPTED UPLINK</h3>
                        <span class="comm-ping">PING: 24ms</span>
                    </div>
                    
                    <div class="comm-input-group">
                        <label class="comm-lbl">ENTER_IDENTIFIER (NAME)</label>
                        <input type="text" id="commName" class="comm-input" placeholder="_type here...">
                    </div>
                    
                    <div class="comm-input-group">
                        <label class="comm-lbl">ENTER_COORDINATES (PHONE)</label>
                        <input type="tel" id="commPhone" class="comm-input" placeholder="_type here...">
                    </div>
                    
                    <div class="comm-input-group">
                        <label class="comm-lbl">TRANSMISSION_PAYLOAD (MESSAGE/COMPLAINT)</label>
                        <textarea id="commMsg" class="comm-input" rows="4" placeholder="_type here..." style="resize:none;"></textarea>

                        <i class="fas fa-paper-plane"></i> TRANSMIT TO HQ
                    </button>

        <script>
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // QQ. DMX Console Engine
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            let strobeInterval = null;

            function updateDMX(channel, val) {
                const env = document.getElementById('dmxConsoleEnv');
                document.getElementById(`dmx-val-${channel}`).innerText = val;
                
                // Update CSS Custom Properties globally for the stage
                if(['r', 'g', 'b'].includes(channel)) {
                    env.style.setProperty(`--dmx-${channel}`, val);
                } else if (channel === 'pan') {
                    env.style.setProperty('--base-pan', `${val}deg`);
                } else if (channel === 'tilt') {
                    env.style.setProperty('--dmx-tilt', `${val}deg`);
                } else if (channel === 'intensity') {
                    // Convert 0-100 to 0.0-1.0
                    env.style.setProperty('--dmx-intensity', val / 100);
                }
            }

            function triggerStrobe() {
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                const env = document.getElementById('dmxConsoleEnv');
                
                if(strobeInterval) {
                    // Stop Strobe
                    clearInterval(strobeInterval);
                    strobeInterval = null;
                    const inten = document.querySelector('.f-int[oninput*="intensity"]').value;
                    env.style.setProperty('--dmx-intensity', inten / 100);
                } else {
                    // Start Strobe (Rapid flicker between 0 and Max)
                    let isOn = false;
                    strobeInterval = setInterval(() => {
                        isOn = !isOn;
                        env.style.setProperty('--dmx-intensity', isOn ? '1' : '0');
                    }, 50); // 50ms = very fast strobe
                }
            }

            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // RR. Generative Event Poster AI (Canvas Engine)
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            const pCanvas = document.getElementById('eventPosterCanvas');
            const pCtx = pCanvas.getContext('2d');
            let currentPosterTheme = 'royal';

            const posterThemes = {
                royal: { bg: '#111', accent: '#D4AF37', textMain: '#fff', fontTitle: 'Cinzel', particle: 'rgba(212,175,55,0.2)' },
                neon: { bg: '#050510', accent: '#ff00ff', textMain: '#00e5ff', fontTitle: 'Orbitron', particle: 'rgba(255,0,255,0.2)' },
                dark: { bg: '#000', accent: '#fff', textMain: '#fff', fontTitle: 'Outfit', particle: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.05)' }
            };

            function setPosterTheme(theme, el) {
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                document.querySelectorAll('.theme-chip').forEach(c => c.classList.remove('active'));
                el.classList.add('active');
                currentPosterTheme = theme;
                drawPoster();
            }

            function drawPoster() {
                const name = document.getElementById('pName').value || 'Event Name';
                const sub = document.getElementById('pSub').value || 'Subtitle';
                const dateRaw = document.getElementById('pDate').value;
                const loc = document.getElementById('pLoc').value || 'Location';
                
                let dateStr = 'DATE NOT SET';
                if(dateRaw) {
                    const d = new Date(dateRaw);
                    dateStr = d.toLocaleDateString('en-IN', { day:'2-digit', month:'long', year:'numeric'}).toUpperCase();
                }

                const t = posterThemes[currentPosterTheme];
                const cw = pCanvas.width;
                const ch = pCanvas.height;

                // 1. Draw Background
                pCtx.fillStyle = t.bg;
                pCtx.fillRect(0, 0, cw, ch);

                // 2. Draw Decorative Elements (Generative Math)
                pCtx.strokeStyle = t.accent;
                pCtx.lineWidth = 2;
                
                if(currentPosterTheme === 'royal') {
                    // Draw classical borders
                    pCtx.strokeRect(40, 40, cw - 80, ch - 80);
                    pCtx.strokeRect(50, 50, cw - 100, ch - 100);
                    // Corner accents
                    pCtx.beginPath(); pCtx.arc(50, 50, 20, 0, 2*Math.PI); pCtx.stroke();
                    pCtx.beginPath(); pCtx.arc(cw-50, 50, 20, 0, 2*Math.PI); pCtx.stroke();
                    pCtx.beginPath(); pCtx.arc(50, ch-50, 20, 0, 2*Math.PI); pCtx.stroke();
                    pCtx.beginPath(); pCtx.arc(cw-50, ch-50, 20, 0, 2*Math.PI); pCtx.stroke();
                } else if(currentPosterTheme === 'neon') {
                    // Draw Cyber grid
                    pCtx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(0,229,255,0.2)';
                    for(let i=0; i<cw; i+=40) { pCtx.beginPath(); pCtx.moveTo(i,0); pCtx.lineTo(i,ch); pCtx.stroke(); }
                    for(let i=0; i<ch; i+=40) { pCtx.beginPath(); pCtx.moveTo(0,i); pCtx.lineTo(cw,i); pCtx.stroke(); }
                    // Triangle focal point
                    pCtx.strokeStyle = t.accent; pCtx.lineWidth = 5;
                    pCtx.beginPath(); pCtx.moveTo(cw/2, 150); pCtx.lineTo(cw-150, ch-200); pCtx.lineTo(150, ch-200); pCtx.closePath(); pCtx.stroke();
                } else {
                    // Minimalist lines
                    pCtx.beginPath(); pCtx.moveTo(cw/2, 50); pCtx.lineTo(cw/2, 150); pCtx.stroke();
                    pCtx.beginPath(); pCtx.moveTo(cw/2, ch-150); pCtx.lineTo(cw/2, ch-50); pCtx.stroke();
                }

                // 3. Draw Typography
                pCtx.textAlign = 'center';
                
                // Top branding
                pCtx.font = `bold 24px 'Outfit'`;
                pCtx.fillStyle = t.accent;
                pCtx.fillText('MAA NIRMALA DJ PRESENTS', cw/2, 120);

                // Main Title (Wrap text if too long)
                pCtx.font = `bold 60px '${t.fontTitle}'`;
                pCtx.fillStyle = t.textMain;
                
                // Shadow for depth
                pCtx.shadowColor = t.accent;
                pCtx.shadowBlur = currentPosterTheme === 'neon' ? 20 : 0;
                
                // Simple centering (In production, use a text-wrap function)
                pCtx.fillText(name.substring(0, 20), cw/2, ch/2 - 50);
                if(name.length > 20) pCtx.fillText(name.substring(20, 40), cw/2, ch/2 + 20);
                
                pCtx.shadowBlur = 0; // Reset shadow

                // Subtitle
                pCtx.font = `30px 'Rajdhani'`;
                pCtx.fillStyle = '#ccc';
                pCtx.fillText(sub, cw/2, ch/2 + 80);

                // Date & Loc
                pCtx.font = `bold 35px 'Outfit'`;
                pCtx.fillStyle = t.accent;
                pCtx.fillText(dateStr, cw/2, ch - 200);
                
                pCtx.font = `25px 'Outfit'`;
                pCtx.fillStyle = '#888';
                pCtx.fillText(loc, cw/2, ch - 150);
            }
            
            // Initial draw
            document.fonts.ready.then(drawPoster); // Wait for web fonts to load

            function downloadPoster() {
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                const loader = document.getElementById('pLoad');
                loader.classList.add('show');
                
                setTimeout(() => {
                    const link = document.createElement('a');
                    link.download = 'MND_Event_Poster.png';
                    link.href = pCanvas.toDataURL('image/png', 1.0);
                    link.click();
                    loader.classList.remove('show');
                    showToast("High-Res Poster Downloaded!");
                }, 800); // Fake render time for premium feel
            }

            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // SS. Secure Comm-Link (Telegram API)
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            function transmitCommLink() {
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                
                const name = document.getElementById('commName').value.trim();
                const phone = document.getElementById('commPhone').value.trim();
                const msgText = document.getElementById('commMsg').value.trim();
                const btn = document.getElementById('commSendBtn');

                if(!name || !phone || !msgText) {
                    showToast("⚠️ ERROR: All telemetry fields required.");
                    return;
                }

                btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-circle-notch fa-spin"></i> ENCRYPTING PAYLOAD...';
                btn.style.pointerEvents = 'none';
                btn.style.color = '#fff';

                const formattedMsg = `📡 *SECURE SATELLITE COMM-LINK* 📡\n---------------------------\n👤 *ID:* ${name}\n📞 *COMMS:* ${phone}\n✉️ *PAYLOAD:*\n_${msgText}_\n\n⏱️ *SYS_TIME:* ${new Date().toLocaleString()}`;

                // Assume TG_TOKEN and TG_CHAT are defined globally in Part 10
                fetch(`https://api.telegram.org/bot${TG_TOKEN}/sendMessage`, { 
                    method: 'POST', 
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, 
                    body: JSON.stringify({ chat_id: TG_CHAT, text: formattedMsg, parse_mode: 'Markdown' }) 
                })
                .then(res => {
                    if(res.ok) {
                        btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-check"></i> TRANSMISSION SUCCESS';
                        btn.style.background = '#00ff00';
                        btn.style.borderColor = '#00ff00';
                        btn.style.color = '#000';
                        showToast("Message securely delivered to HQ.");
                        
                        // Reset Form
                        setTimeout(() => {
                            document.getElementById('commName').value = '';
                            document.getElementById('commPhone').value = '';
                            document.getElementById('commMsg').value = '';
                            btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-paper-plane"></i> TRANSMIT TO HQ';
                            btn.style.background = 'transparent';
                            btn.style.borderColor = '#00e5ff';
                            btn.style.color = '#00e5ff';
                            btn.style.pointerEvents = 'auto';
                        }, 3000);
                    } else { throw new Error('Network response was not ok.'); }
                })
                .catch(err => {
                    btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-times"></i> TRANSMISSION FAILED';
                    btn.style.background = '#ff3333';
                    btn.style.borderColor = '#ff3333';
                    btn.style.color = '#fff';
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-paper-plane"></i> RETRY TRANSMISSION';
                        btn.style.background = 'transparent';
                        btn.style.borderColor = '#00e5ff';
                        btn.style.color = '#00e5ff';
                        btn.style.pointerEvents = 'auto';
                    }, 3000);
                });
            }
        </script>

        <div class="showcase-container reveal-on-scroll">
            <h2 class="section-label-pro"><i class="fas fa-route"></i> AI EVENT JOURNEY MAPPER</h2>
            <p style="text-align: center; color: var(--text-sub); font-family: 'Outfit'; font-size: 13px; margin-top:-15px;">Visualize the acoustic energy flow of your standard event timeline.</p>

                <div style="display:flex; justify-content:center; gap:10px;">
                    <button class="cc-btn" style="width:auto; padding:0 20px; border-radius:30px; font-family:'Rajdhani'; font-size:12px;" onclick="generateJourney('wedding')">WEDDING</button>
                    <button class="cc-btn" style="width:auto; padding:0 20px; border-radius:30px; font-family:'Rajdhani'; font-size:12px;" onclick="generateJourney('club')">CLUB NIGHT</button>
                </div>

                <div class="journey-graph-container" id="journeyGraph">
                    <svg id="journeyLineSvg"><path id="jPath" fill="none" stroke="rgba(255,255,255,0.2)" stroke-width="2" stroke-dasharray="5,5"/></svg>
                    </div>
            </div>
        </div>

        <script>
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // TT. Biometric Client Vault Logic
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            let scanTimer = null;
            let scanProgress = 0;
            const scanCircle = document.getElementById('scanProgress');
            const maxOffset = 502;
            const laser = document.getElementById('scanLaser');
            const fpIcon = document.getElementById('fpIcon');
            const statusTxt = document.getElementById('scanStatus');
            let isUnlocked = false;

            function startScan(e) {
                if(isUnlocked) return;
                e.preventDefault(); // Prevent text selection/magnifier on mobile
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                
                statusTxt.innerText = "ANALYZING BIOMETRICS...";
                statusTxt.style.color = "#00e5ff";
                fpIcon.style.color = "#00e5ff";
                laser.style.opacity = '1';
                
                // Animate Laser scanning up and down
                laser.style.animation = 'scanUpDown 0.5s linear infinite alternate';
                
                scanTimer = setInterval(() => {
                    scanProgress += 2; // Speed of unlock
                    const currentOffset = maxOffset - ((scanProgress / 100) * maxOffset);
                    scanCircle.style.strokeDashoffset = currentOffset;
                    
                    if(scanProgress >= 100) {
                        unlockVault();
                    }
                }, 30);
            }

            function stopScan(e) {
                if(isUnlocked) return;
                e.preventDefault();
                clearInterval(scanTimer);
                scanProgress = 0;
                scanCircle.style.strokeDashoffset = maxOffset; // Reset ring
                
                statusTxt.innerText = "SCAN ABORTED.";
                statusTxt.style.color = "var(--accent-red)";
                fpIcon.style.color = "rgba(0, 229, 255, 0.5)";
                laser.style.opacity = '0';
                laser.style.animation = 'none';
                
                setTimeout(() => { if(!isUnlocked) { statusTxt.innerText = "AWAITING INPUT..."; statusTxt.style.color = "var(--gold-primary)"; }}, 1000);
            }

            function unlockVault() {
                clearInterval(scanTimer);
                isUnlocked = true;
                if(navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate([100, 50, 100]);
                
                document.getElementById('vaultAuthUI').style.display = 'none';
                document.getElementById('vaultData').style.display = 'block';
                if(engineOn) enginePlay('laserA'); // Play success sound
            }

            function lockVault() {
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                isUnlocked = false;
                scanProgress = 0;
                scanCircle.style.strokeDashoffset = maxOffset;
                document.getElementById('vaultAuthUI').style.display = 'block';
                document.getElementById('vaultData').style.display = 'none';
                statusTxt.innerText = "VAULT SECURED.";
                setTimeout(() => { statusTxt.innerText = "AWAITING INPUT..."; }, 2000);
            }

            // CSS Animation for laser (injected dynamically)
            const styleSheet = document.createElement("style");
            styleSheet.innerText = `@keyframes scanUpDown { 0% { top: 10px; } 100% { top: 130px; } }`;
            document.head.appendChild(styleSheet);

            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // UU. Acoustic Room Analyzer (Web Audio API Mic Input)
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            let micStream = null;
            let micCtx = null;
            let micAnalyser = null;
            let micDataArray = null;
            let mCanvas = document.getElementById('micCanvas');
            let mCtx = mCanvas.getContext('2d');
            let mAnimFrame = null;
            let isMicActive = false;

            async function initRoomAnalyzer() {
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                const btn = document.getElementById('btnMicInit');
                const verdict = document.getElementById('micVerdict');
                
                if(!isMicActive) {
                    try {
                        btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-spinner fa-spin"></i> CONNECTING...';
                        
                        micStream = await navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia({ audio: true, video: false });
                        
                        const AudioContext = window.AudioContext || window.webkitAudioContext;
                        micCtx = new AudioContext();
                        const source = micCtx.createMediaStreamSource(micStream);
                        
                        micAnalyser = micCtx.createAnalyser();
                        micAnalyser.fftSize = 256;
                        source.connect(micAnalyser);
                        // Do NOT connect to destination, or it will create a feedback loop!
                        
                        micDataArray = new Uint8Array(micAnalyser.frequencyBinCount);
                        
                        // Setup Canvas
                        const rect = mCanvas.parentElement.getBoundingClientRect();
                        mCanvas.width = rect.width; mCanvas.height = rect.height;
                        
                        isMicActive = true;
                        btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-stop"></i> STOP SCAN';
                        btn.style.color = '#ff3333'; btn.style.borderColor = '#ff3333';
                        
                        analyzeRoomAudio();
                        showToast("Acoustic Sensors Online.");
                        
                    } catch(err) {
                        console.error("Mic Error:", err);
                        btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-exclamation-triangle"></i> ACCESS DENIED';
                        verdict.innerHTML = "<strong style='color:#ff3333;'>ERROR:</strong> Microphone permission denied. Cannot analyze room acoustics.";
                        setTimeout(() => { btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-rss"></i> INIT HARDWARE MIC'; }, 3000);
                    }
                } else {
                    // Stop Mic
                    isMicActive = false;
                    if(micStream) micStream.getTracks().forEach(track => track.stop());
                    if(micCtx) micCtx.close();
                    if(mAnimFrame) cancelAnimationFrame(mAnimFrame);
                    
                    mCtx.clearRect(0, 0, mCanvas.width, mCanvas.height);
                    document.getElementById('dbReadout').innerText = '--';
                    document.getElementById('dbReadout').style.color = '#00ff00';
                    btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-rss"></i> INIT HARDWARE MIC';
                    btn.style.color = '#00e5ff'; btn.style.borderColor = '#00e5ff';
                    verdict.innerHTML = "<strong>SCAN HALTED.</strong>";
                }
            }

            function analyzeRoomAudio() {
                if(!isMicActive) return;
                mAnimFrame = requestAnimationFrame(analyzeRoomAudio);
                
                micAnalyser.getByteFrequencyData(micDataArray);
                
                // Calculate rough Decibel (dB) equivalent from frequency data
                let sum = 0;
                for(let i=0; i<micDataArray.length; i++) { sum += micDataArray[i]; }
                const average = sum / micDataArray.length;
                
                // Map average (0-255) to a fake dB range (30 quiet room - 120 concert) for visual effect
                const db = Math.floor(30 + (average / 255) * 90); 
                const dbDisplay = document.getElementById('dbReadout');
                dbDisplay.innerText = db;
                
                const verdict = document.getElementById('micVerdict');

                // Color coding and verdict logic based on dB
                if(db < 50) {
                    dbDisplay.style.color = '#00e5ff'; // Cyan
                    verdict.innerHTML = "<strong>VERDICT: TOO QUIET.</strong> Absolute silence detected. The venue desperately requires an MND Heavy DJ deployment to generate atmospheric energy.";
                } else if(db < 85) {
                    dbDisplay.style.color = '#00ff00'; // Green
                    verdict.innerHTML = "<strong>VERDICT: AMBIENT LEVEL.</strong> Normal conversation detected. MND Line-Array speakers recommended to overpower crowd noise.";
                } else {
                    dbDisplay.style.color = '#ff3333'; // Red
                    dbDisplay.style.textShadow = '0 0 20px rgba(255,0,0,0.8)';
                    verdict.innerHTML = "<strong>VERDICT: ACOUSTIC SATURATION.</strong> Environment is loud. Maximum 21-inch Subwoofer arrays required to penetrate the noise floor.";
                }

                // Draw Spectrum on Canvas
                mCtx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.2)'; // fade effect
                mCtx.fillRect(0, 0, mCanvas.width, mCanvas.height);
                
                const barWidth = (mCanvas.width / micDataArray.length) * 2.5;
                let barHeight;
                let x = 0;
                
                for(let i = 0; i < micDataArray.length; i++) {
                    barHeight = (micDataArray[i] / 255) * mCanvas.height;
                    
                    // Color gradient based on frequency
                    const r = barHeight + (25 * (i/micDataArray.length));
                    const g = 250 * (i/micDataArray.length);
                    const b = 255;
                    
                    mCtx.fillStyle = `rgb(${r},${g},${b})`;
                    mCtx.fillRect(x, mCanvas.height - barHeight, barWidth, barHeight);
                    x += barWidth + 1;
                }
            }

            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // VV. AI Setlist Journey Mapper Logic
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            const jGraph = document.getElementById('journeyGraph');
            const jPath = document.getElementById('jPath');

            const journeyData = {
                wedding: [
                    { time: '18:00', lbl: 'Warmup', class: 'e-low', desc: 'Soft instrumental background.' },
                    { time: '19:30', lbl: 'Baraat', class: 'e-high', desc: 'Max bass, heavy Dhol tracks.' },
                    { time: '21:00', lbl: 'Varmala', class: 'e-mid', desc: 'Cinematic entries, fog machines.' },
                    { time: '22:30', lbl: 'Dinner', class: 'e-low', desc: 'Classic melodies, low volume.' },
                    { time: '00:00', lbl: 'Dance', class: 'e-high', desc: 'Full club energy, EDM/Bollywood.' }
                ],
                club: [
                    { time: '20:00', lbl: 'Doors', class: 'e-low', desc: 'Deep house, building tension.' },
                    { time: '22:00', lbl: 'Groove', class: 'e-mid', desc: 'Tech house, lasers active.' },
                    { time: '00:00', lbl: 'Peak', class: 'e-high', desc: 'Big room anthems, strobe max.' },
                    { time: '02:00', lbl: 'Drop', class: 'e-high', desc: 'Heavy bassline drops.' },
                    { time: '04:00', lbl: 'Close', class: 'e-mid', desc: 'Euphoric trance exit.' }
                ]
            };

            function generateJourney(type) {
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                
                // Clear existing nodes (except SVG)
                const nodes = jGraph.querySelectorAll('.journey-node');
                nodes.forEach(n => n.remove());

                const data = journeyData[type];
                let pathD = "";
                let xOffset = 60; // Start padding

                data.forEach((item, index) => {
                    const node = document.createElement('div');
                    node.className = 'journey-node';
                    node.style.animation = `slideInUp 0.5s ${index * 0.1}s backwards`;
                    
                    node.innerHTML = `
                        <span class="j-time">${item.time}</span>
                        <div class="j-bar ${item.class}"></div>
                        <span class="j-lbl">${item.lbl}</span>
                        <div class="j-tooltip">${item.desc}</div>
                    `;
                    
                    jGraph.appendChild(node);

                    // Calculate path for SVG line connecting the tops of the bars
                    // Height values mapped from classes (low:40, mid:100, high:160)
                    let h = item.class === 'e-low' ? 40 : item.class === 'e-mid' ? 100 : 160;
                    // Y position from top of container (Container height 250 - padding 20 - bar height)
                    let yPos = 250 - 20 - h; 
                    
                    if(index === 0) pathD += `M ${xOffset} ${yPos} `;
                    else pathD += `L ${xOffset} ${yPos} `;
                    
                    xOffset += 72; // Bar width (12) + margin-right (60)
                });

                // Update SVG Line
                jPath.setAttribute('d', pathD);
                
                // Animate the line drawing
                jPath.style.strokeDasharray = jPath.getTotalLength();
                jPath.style.strokeDashoffset = jPath.getTotalLength();
                setTimeout(() => {
                    jPath.style.transition = 'stroke-dashoffset 1.5s ease-in-out';
                    jPath.style.strokeDashoffset = 0;
                }, 100);
            }

            // Init default journey
            generateJourney('wedding');
        </script>

        <style>
            .hex-grid-wrapper {

        <div class="showcase-container reveal-on-scroll">
            <h2 class="section-label-pro"><i class="fas fa-spider"></i> COMPETITIVE HEX-METRICS</h2>
            
            <div class="hex-grid-wrapper">
                <div class="hex-canvas-box">

        <script>
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // WW. Spatial Audio Simulator Logic
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            const sRoom = document.getElementById('sRoom');
            const sListener = document.getElementById('sListener');
            const sStage = document.getElementById('sStage');
            
            let isSpatialDragging = false;

            sListener.addEventListener('mousedown', () => isSpatialDragging = true);
            sListener.addEventListener('touchstart', (e) => { isSpatialDragging = true; e.preventDefault(); }, {passive: false});

            window.addEventListener('mouseup', () => isSpatialDragging = false);
            window.addEventListener('touchend', () => isSpatialDragging = false);

            window.addEventListener('mousemove', handleSpatialDrag);
            window.addEventListener('touchmove', handleSpatialDrag, {passive: false});

            function handleSpatialDrag(e) {
                if(!isSpatialDragging) return;
                e.preventDefault();

                const rect = sRoom.getBoundingClientRect();
                const clientX = e.type.includes('touch') ? e.touches[0].clientX : e.clientX;
                const clientY = e.type.includes('touch') ? e.touches[0].clientY : e.clientY;

                let x = clientX - rect.left;
                let y = clientY - rect.top;

                // Clamp to room boundaries
                if(x < 20) x = 20; if(x > rect.width - 20) x = rect.width - 20;
                if(y < 60) y = 60; if(y > rect.height - 20) y = rect.height - 20;

                sListener.style.left = `${x}px`;
                sListener.style.top = `${y}px`;

                calculateAcoustics(x, y, rect.width, rect.height);
            }

            function calculateAcoustics(lx, ly, w, h) {
                // Stage is top center
                const sx = w / 2;
                const sy = 20;

                // Calculate Distance (Pythagorean)
                const dx = lx - sx;
                const dy = ly - sy;
                const distancePx = Math.sqrt(dx*dx + dy*dy);
                
                // Convert px to virtual meters (e.g., max height is 30m)
                const distanceM = (distancePx / h) * 30;
                document.getElementById('sDistVal').innerText = distanceM.toFixed(1);

                // Calculate Panning (-1 to 1) based on X axis
                const pan = (dx / (w/2)).toFixed(2);
                let panText = "CENTER";
                if(pan < -0.1) panText = `L ${(Math.abs(pan)*100).toFixed(0)}%`;
                else if (pan > 0.1) panText = `R ${(pan*100).toFixed(0)}%`;
                document.getElementById('sPanVal').innerText = panText;

                // Calculate Volume Drop (Inverse square law approximation)
                // Max SPL near stage = 140dB. Drops by 6dB every doubling of distance.
                let spl = 140 - (Math.log2(distanceM > 1 ? distanceM : 1) * 6);
                if(spl > 140) spl = 140;
                
                const volEl = document.getElementById('sVolVal');
                volEl.innerText = `${spl.toFixed(1)} dB`;
                
                if(spl > 120) volEl.style.color = '#ff3333';
                else if(spl > 100) volEl.style.color = '#ffff00';
                else volEl.style.color = '#00ff00';

                // Optional: Hook this into Web Audio PannerNode if audio engine is running
                /*
                if(engineOn && proCtx && pannerNode) {
                    pannerNode.positionX.value = pan;
                    pannerNode.positionZ.value = distanceM / 30; // 0 to 1 depth
                }
                */
            }

            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // XX. Pyrotechnic Trajectory Engine (Canvas + Timeline)
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            const pyroCanvas = document.getElementById('pyroCanvas');
            const pyCtx = pyroCanvas.getContext('2d');
            const pTimeline = document.getElementById('pTimeline');
            const pScrubber = document.getElementById('pScrubber');
            
            let pyroNodes = []; // { xPct: 0-100 }
            let isPyroPlaying = false;
            let pyroTime = 0; // 0 to 100 (percentage of timeline)
            let particlesPyro = [];
            let pyroAnimFrame = null;

            function resizePyro() {
                const rect = pyroCanvas.parentElement.getBoundingClientRect();
                pyroCanvas.width = rect.width; pyroCanvas.height = rect.height;
            }
            window.addEventListener('resize', resizePyro);
            resizePyro();

            function addPyroNode(e) {
                if(isPyroPlaying) return;
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                
                const rect = pTimeline.getBoundingClientRect();
                const x = e.clientX - rect.left;
                const xPct = (x / rect.width) * 100;
                
                pyroNodes.push({ xPct, triggered: false, el: null });
                
                // Create DOM element for visual
                const nodeEl = document.createElement('div');
                nodeEl.className = 'pyro-node';
                nodeEl.style.left = `${xPct}%`;
                pTimeline.appendChild(nodeEl);
                pyroNodes[pyroNodes.length-1].el = nodeEl;
            }

            function clearPyroNodes() {
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                pyroNodes.forEach(n => n.el.remove());
                pyroNodes = [];
                particlesPyro = [];
                pyCtx.clearRect(0,0, pyroCanvas.width, pyroCanvas.height);
                pyroTime = 0;
                pScrubber.style.left = '0%';
                if(isPyroPlaying) togglePyroSequence();
            }

            function togglePyroSequence() {
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                const btn = document.getElementById('btnPlayPyro');
                
                if(!isPyroPlaying) {
                    isPyroPlaying = true;
                    btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-stop"></i> ABORT';
                    btn.style.background = '#222'; btn.style.color = '#ff3333';
                    
                    // Reset nodes
                    pyroNodes.forEach(n => { n.triggered = false; n.el.classList.remove('triggered'); });
                    pyroTime = 0;
                    animatePyroSystem();
                } else {
                    isPyroPlaying = false;
                    btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-play"></i> LAUNCH SEQUENCE';
                    btn.style.background = '#ff3333'; btn.style.color = '#fff';
                    if(pyroAnimFrame) cancelAnimationFrame(pyroAnimFrame);
                }
            }

            class Spark {
                constructor(x, y, color) {
                    this.x = x; this.y = y;
                    const angle = Math.random() * Math.PI * 2;
                    const speed = Math.random() * 8 + 4;
                    this.vx = Math.cos(angle) * speed;
                    this.vy = Math.sin(angle) * speed;
                    this.life = 1.0;
                    this.decay = Math.random() * 0.02 + 0.015;
                    this.color = color;
                    this.size = Math.random() * 3 + 1;
                }
                update() {
                    this.vy += 0.2; // Gravity
                    this.vx *= 0.95; // Friction
                    this.vy *= 0.95;
                    this.x += this.vx; this.y += this.vy;
                    this.life -= this.decay;
                }
                draw(ctx) {
                    ctx.globalAlpha = this.life;
                    ctx.fillStyle = this.color;
                    ctx.shadowBlur = 10; ctx.shadowColor = this.color;
                    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(this.x, this.y, this.size, 0, Math.PI*2); ctx.fill();
                    ctx.globalAlpha = 1; ctx.shadowBlur = 0;
                }
            }

            function launchFirework() {
                // Launch from stage (bottom center)
                const startX = (pyroCanvas.width / 2) + (Math.random() * 100 - 50);
                const startY = pyroCanvas.height;
                const colors = ['#ff3333', '#FFD700', '#00e5ff', '#fff'];
                const c = colors[Math.floor(Math.random() * colors.length)];
                
                if(navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate(50);
                
                // Explode higher up
                const explodeY = Math.random() * (pyroCanvas.height / 2) + 20;
                
                for(let i=0; i<40; i++) {
                    particlesPyro.push(new Spark(startX, explodeY, c));
                }
                
                // Flash the canvas
                pyCtx.fillStyle = 'rgba(255,255,255,0.3)';
                pyCtx.fillRect(0,0, pyroCanvas.width, pyroCanvas.height);
            }

            function animatePyroSystem() {
                if(!isPyroPlaying) return;
                pyroAnimFrame = requestAnimationFrame(animatePyroSystem);
                
                // Timeline logic
                pyroTime += 0.4; // Speed of scrubber
                if(pyroTime > 100) { togglePyroSequence(); return; } // End sequence
                
                pScrubber.style.left = `${pyroTime}%`;
                
                // Check nodes
                pyroNodes.forEach(n => {
                    if(!n.triggered && pyroTime >= n.xPct) {
                        n.triggered = true;
                        n.el.classList.add('triggered');
                        launchFirework();
                    }
                });
                
                // Render Canvas
                pyCtx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.2)'; // fade tail
                pyCtx.fillRect(0, 0, pyroCanvas.width, pyroCanvas.height);
                
                pyCtx.globalCompositeOperation = 'lighter';
                for(let i = particlesPyro.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
                    const p = particlesPyro[i];
                    p.update();
                    p.draw(pyCtx);
                    if(p.life <= 0) particlesPyro.splice(i, 1);
                }
                pyCtx.globalCompositeOperation = 'source-over';
            }

            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // YY. Hex-Grid Performance Analytics (Canvas Radar Chart)
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            const hexCanvas = document.getElementById('hexCanvas');
            const hCtx = hexCanvas.getContext('2d');
            let hexAnimOffset = 0;

            function initHex() {
                // Fix DPI for crisp text
                const dpr = window.devicePixelRatio || 1;
                hexCanvas.width = 300 * dpr;
                hexCanvas.height = 300 * dpr;
                hCtx.scale(dpr, dpr);
                drawHexChart();
            }
            window.addEventListener('resize', initHex);
            
            // Data points (0 to 100)
            const mndData = [95, 90, 100, 95, 85, 90];
            const stdData = [60, 40, 50, 60, 70, 50];

            function drawPolygon(cx, cy, radius, sides, ctx, strokeStyle, fillStyle) {
                ctx.beginPath();
                for (let i = 0; i < sides; i++) {
                    // Start at top (-PI/2)
                    const angle = (Math.PI * 2 * i) / sides - Math.PI / 2;
                    const x = cx + radius * Math.cos(angle);
                    const y = cy + radius * Math.sin(angle);
                    if (i === 0) ctx.moveTo(x, y);
                    else ctx.lineTo(x, y);
                }
                ctx.closePath();
                if(fillStyle) { ctx.fillStyle = fillStyle; ctx.fill(); }
                if(strokeStyle) { ctx.strokeStyle = strokeStyle; ctx.stroke(); }
            }

            function drawDataPolygon(cx, cy, maxRadius, dataArr, ctx, color, isGlowing) {
                ctx.beginPath();
                for (let i = 0; i < 6; i++) {
                    const angle = (Math.PI * 2 * i) / 6 - Math.PI / 2;
                    // Add slight sine wave animation to the data points for a "live" feel
                    const animVariance = isGlowing ? Math.sin(hexAnimOffset + i) * 2 : 0;
                    const val = dataArr[i] + animVariance;
                    
                    const r = (val / 100) * maxRadius;
                    const x = cx + r * Math.cos(angle);
                    const y = cy + r * Math.sin(angle);
                    
                    if (i === 0) ctx.moveTo(x, y);
                    else ctx.lineTo(x, y);
                }
                ctx.closePath();
                
                if(isGlowing) {
                    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(212,175,55,0.3)';
                    ctx.shadowBlur = 15; ctx.shadowColor = color;
                } else {
                    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(100,100,100,0.2)';
                    ctx.shadowBlur = 0;
                }
                
                ctx.fill();
                ctx.lineWidth = 2;
                ctx.strokeStyle = color;
                ctx.stroke();
                ctx.shadowBlur = 0; // reset
            }

            function drawHexChart() {
                requestAnimationFrame(drawHexChart);
                hexAnimOffset += 0.05;

                const cx = 150; const cy = 150; const maxR = 120;
                hCtx.clearRect(0,0, 300, 300);

                // Draw Background Web
                hCtx.lineWidth = 1;
                for(let i=1; i<=5; i++) {
                    drawPolygon(cx, cy, maxR * (i/5), 6, hCtx, 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)', null);
                }
                
                // Draw Spokes
                hCtx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)';
                for (let i = 0; i < 6; i++) {
                    const angle = (Math.PI * 2 * i) / 6 - Math.PI / 2;
                    hCtx.beginPath(); hCtx.moveTo(cx, cy);
                    hCtx.lineTo(cx + maxR * Math.cos(angle), cy + maxR * Math.sin(angle));
                    hCtx.stroke();
                }

                // Draw Standard Competitor Data
                drawDataPolygon(cx, cy, maxR, stdData, hCtx, '#666', false);
                // Draw MND Premium Data
                drawDataPolygon(cx, cy, maxR, mndData, hCtx, '#D4AF37', true);
            }
            
            // Need a slight delay to ensure fonts/layout are ready
            setTimeout(initHex, 500);
        </script>

            .map-interface {

            /* Topographic Map Lines */

                                  radial-gradient(circle at 80% 70%, transparent 30%, #002233 31%, transparent 32%);

            #routeSvg { position: absolute; inset: 0; width: 100%; height: 100%; z-index: 2; }
            
            /* Animated Tractor Blip */
            .tractor-blip {

                color: #ffcc00; font-size: 12px; z-index: 5;

            }
            .tractor-blip::after { content:''; position:absolute; width:40px; height:40px; border:1px solid #ffcc00; border-radius:50%; animation: radarPulse 2s infinite; }

            .map-node {
                position: absolute; width: 12px; height: 12px; background: #fff; border-radius: 50%;
                transform: translate(-50%, -50%); z-index: 3; box-shadow: 0 0 10px #fff;
            }
            .map-node-lbl { position: absolute; color: #fff; font-family: 'Rajdhani'; font-size: 10px; font-weight: bold; transform: translateX(-50%); margin-top: 10px; z-index: 4;}

            .telemetry-stats {
                display: grid; grid-template-columns: repeat(3, 1fr); gap: 10px; margin-top: 15px;
            }
            .t-stat-box { background: rgba(255,255,255,0.05); border: 1px solid #333; border-radius: 8px; padding: 10px; text-align: center; }
            .t-lbl { display: block; font-family: 'Orbitron'; font-size: 9px; color: #00e5ff; letter-spacing: 1px; margin-bottom: 5px; }
            .t-val { font-family: 'Outfit'; font-size: 16px; color: #fff; font-weight: 900; }
        </style>

        <div class="showcase-container reveal-on-scroll">
            <h2 class="section-label-pro"><i class="fas fa-truck-moving"></i> LAXMIKANT FLEET TELEMETRY</h2>
            <p style="text-align: center; color: var(--text-sub); font-family: 'Outfit'; font-size: 13px; margin-top:-15px;">Live logistics tracking for heavy equipment dispatch.</p>

            <div class="telemetry-wrapper">
                <div class="map-interface" id="mapEnv">
                    <svg id="routeSvg">
                        <path id="deliveryRoute" fill="none" stroke="rgba(0, 229, 255, 0.4)" stroke-width="3" stroke-dasharray="8,8"/>
                    </svg>
                    
                    <div class="map-node" id="nodeHQ" style="background:var(--gold-primary); box-shadow:0 0 15px var(--gold-primary);"></div>
                    <div class="map-node-lbl" id="lblHQ">BELTIKRI HQ</div>
                    
                    <div class="map-node" id="nodeDest" style="background:#00e5ff;"></div>
                    <div class="map-node-lbl" id="lblDest">VENUE DROP</div>

                    <div class="tractor-blip" id="tractorIcon"><i class="fas fa-tractor"></i></div>
                </div>

                <div class="telemetry-stats">
                    <div class="t-stat-box">
                        <span class="t-lbl">PAYLOAD WT</span>
                        <span class="t-val">8.5 TON</span>
                    </div>
                    <div class="t-stat-box">
                        <span class="t-lbl">TERRAIN</span>
                        <span class="t-val" style="color:var(--gold-shine);">OFF-ROAD</span>
                    </div>
                    <div class="t-stat-box">
                        <span class="t-lbl">SYS ETA</span>
                        <span class="t-val" id="etaTracker">14:30</span>
                    </div>
                </div>

                <button class="f-btn" style="margin-top: 15px; background: #111; color: #00e5ff; border: 1px solid #00e5ff;" onclick="startDelivery()">
                    <i class="fas fa-satellite"></i> DISPATCH HEAVY TRACTOR
                </button>
            </div>
        </div>

        <script>
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // ZZ. DG Set Load Balancer Logic
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            let dualSyncEnabled = false;
            let isBlackout = false;
            const singleGenMax = 60; // kW limit for one generator
            const dualGenMax = 120;

            function calcPowerLoad() {
                if(isBlackout) return; // Frozen during blackout

                const a = parseInt(document.getElementById('ldAudio').value);
                const l = parseInt(document.getElementById('ldLights').value);
                const c = parseInt(document.getElementById('ldCater').value);
                
                document.getElementById('valAudio').innerText = a;
                document.getElementById('valLights').innerText = l;
                document.getElementById('valCater').innerText = c;

                const totalKw = a + l + c;
                const kwDisplay = document.getElementById('currentKwVal');
                const bar = document.getElementById('loadBarFill');
                const limitLine = document.getElementById('loadLimitLine');

                kwDisplay.innerText = `${totalKw} kW`;
                
                // Max visual width is currently based on either 100kW or 150kW
                const visualMax = dualSyncEnabled ? 150 : 100;
                let pct = (totalKw / visualMax) * 100;
                if(pct > 100) pct = 100;
                bar.style.width = `${pct}%`;

                // Update limit line position visually
                const limitKw = dualSyncEnabled ? dualGenMax : singleGenMax;
                limitLine.style.left = `${(limitKw / visualMax) * 100}%`;

                // Color warning
                if(totalKw > limitKw * 0.8) {
                    kwDisplay.style.color = '#ffff00'; // Warning yellow
                } else {
                    kwDisplay.style.color = '#00ff00';
                }

                // Blackout Trigger Logic
                if(totalKw >= limitKw) {
                    triggerBlackout();
                }
            }

            function triggerBlackout() {
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                if(navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate([500, 200, 500]);
                isBlackout = true;
                
                const env = document.getElementById('powerGridEnv');
                env.classList.add('blackout');
                
                // Reset sliders visually
                document.getElementById('ldAudio').value = 0;
                document.getElementById('ldLights').value = 0;
                document.getElementById('ldCater').value = 0;
                document.getElementById('valAudio').innerText = 0;
                document.getElementById('valLights').innerText = 0;
                document.getElementById('valCater').innerText = 0;
                document.getElementById('currentKwVal').innerText = "FAIL";
                document.getElementById('currentKwVal').style.color = "#ff3333";
                document.getElementById('loadBarFill').style.width = "0%";
                
                // Shut down audio engine if running
                if(engineOn) toggleAudioEngine();
            }

            function resetBreaker() {
                if(!isBlackout) return;
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                isBlackout = false;
                document.getElementById('powerGridEnv').classList.remove('blackout');
                calcPowerLoad(); // Recalculate with reset sliders
                showToast("System Reset. Monitor Load.");
            }

            function toggleDualSync() {
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                const btn = document.getElementById('btnSyncGen');
                
                dualSyncEnabled = !dualSyncEnabled;
                
                if(dualSyncEnabled) {
                    btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-link"></i> DUAL-SYNC ACTIVE';
                    btn.style.background = 'linear-gradient(180deg, #00ff00, #009900)';
                    btn.style.borderColor = '#004400';
                    document.querySelector('.gen-title').innerText = "DG SET A + B (SYNCED)";
                    document.querySelector('.gen-title').nextElementSibling.innerText = "125 kVA Total Output";
                    showToast("Secondary Generator Online. Max Limit Increased to 120kW.");
                } else {
                    btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-link"></i> ENGAGE DUAL-SYNC';
                    btn.style.background = 'linear-gradient(180deg, #00e5ff, #007799)';
                    btn.style.borderColor = '#003344';
                    document.querySelector('.gen-title').innerText = "SILENT DG SET A";
                    document.querySelector('.gen-title').nextElementSibling.innerText = "62.5 kVA Kirloskar Core";
                    showToast("Running on Single Phase.");
                }
                
                calcPowerLoad();
            }

            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // AAA. Line Array J-Curve Rigging Logic
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            const rCanvas = document.getElementById('rigCanvas');
            const rCtx = rCanvas.getContext('2d');

            function resizeRig() {
                const rect = rCanvas.parentElement.getBoundingClientRect();
                rCanvas.width = rect.width; rCanvas.height = rect.height;
                drawRig();
            }
            window.addEventListener('resize', resizeRig);
            
            function drawRig() {
                if(!rCtx) return;
                rCtx.clearRect(0,0, rCanvas.width, rCanvas.height);

                const a1 = parseInt(document.getElementById('ang1').value);
                const a2 = parseInt(document.getElementById('ang2').value);
                const a3 = parseInt(document.getElementById('ang3').value);
                const a4 = parseInt(document.getElementById('ang4').value);

                document.getElementById('angVal1').innerText = `${a1}°`;
                document.getElementById('angVal2').innerText = `${a2}°`;
                document.getElementById('angVal3').innerText = `${a3}°`;
                document.getElementById('angVal4').innerText = `${a4}°`;

                // Truss / Bumper position
                const startX = 50; const startY = 20;
                
                rCtx.save();
                rCtx.translate(startX, startY);

                // Draw Chain Hoist
                rCtx.strokeStyle = '#555'; rCtx.lineWidth = 4;
                rCtx.beginPath(); rCtx.moveTo(0,-20); rCtx.lineTo(0,0); rCtx.stroke();

                // Array mechanics
                const boxH = 30; const boxW = 40;
                const angles = [a1, a2, a3, a4];
                let currentTotalAngle = 0; // Cumulative angle for rigging

                angles.forEach((ang, idx) => {
                    currentTotalAngle += ang;
                    // Convert degrees to radians for drawing
                    const rad = currentTotalAngle * (Math.PI / 180);
                    
                    rCtx.rotate(rad);
                    
                    // Draw Box
                    rCtx.fillStyle = '#222'; rCtx.strokeStyle = '#555'; rCtx.lineWidth = 2;
                    rCtx.fillRect(-boxW/2, 0, boxW, boxH);
                    rCtx.strokeRect(-boxW/2, 0, boxW, boxH);
                    
                    // Draw Acoustic Beam (Throw)
                    rCtx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0, 229, 255, 0.15)';
                    rCtx.beginPath();
                    // Beam originates from center of box face
                    rCtx.moveTo(boxW/2, boxH/2);
                    // Draw a long wedge
                    rCtx.lineTo(800, -100);
                    rCtx.lineTo(800, boxH + 100);
                    rCtx.closePath();
                    rCtx.fill();

                    // Move down for next box
                    rCtx.translate(0, boxH + 2); 
                    // Reverse rotation so next box calculates angle relative to this one
                    rCtx.rotate(-rad); 
                });

                rCtx.restore();
            }
            
            // Init canvas properly
            setTimeout(resizeRig, 100);

            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // BBB. Laxmikant Fleet Telemetry Tracker Logic
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            const mapEnv = document.getElementById('mapEnv');
            const routeSvg = document.getElementById('routeSvg');
            const deliveryRoute = document.getElementById('deliveryRoute');
            const nodeHQ = document.getElementById('nodeHQ');
            const nodeDest = document.getElementById('nodeDest');
            const lblHQ = document.getElementById('lblHQ');
            const lblDest = document.getElementById('lblDest');
            const tractor = document.getElementById('tractorIcon');
            
            let isDelivering = false;
            let deliveryProgress = 0;
            let deliveryTimer = null;

            function setupMap() {
                const w = mapEnv.clientWidth;
                const h = mapEnv.clientHeight;
                
                // Define Points
                const hqX = 40; const hqY = h - 40; // Bottom Left
                const destX = w - 40; const destY = 40; // Top Right
                
                // Place DOM Nodes
                nodeHQ.style.left = `${hqX}px`; nodeHQ.style.top = `${hqY}px`;
                lblHQ.style.left = `${hqX}px`; lblHQ.style.top = `${hqY}px`;
                
                nodeDest.style.left = `${destX}px`; nodeDest.style.top = `${destY}px`;
                lblDest.style.left = `${destX}px`; lblDest.style.top = `${destY}px`;

                // Draw SVG bezier curve
                const cp1X = w * 0.3; const cp1Y = h * 0.2; // Control Point 1
                const cp2X = w * 0.7; const cp2Y = h * 0.8; // Control Point 2
                
                const pathStr = `M ${hqX} ${hqY} C ${cp1X} ${cp1Y}, ${cp2X} ${cp2Y}, ${destX} ${destY}`;
                deliveryRoute.setAttribute('d', pathStr);
                
                // Initial Tractor position
                if(!isDelivering) {
                    tractor.style.left = `${hqX}px`;
                    tractor.style.top = `${hqY}px`;
                }
            }
            window.addEventListener('resize', setupMap);
            setTimeout(setupMap, 100);

            function startDelivery() {
                if(isDelivering) return;
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                
                isDelivering = true;
                deliveryProgress = 0;
                const pathLength = deliveryRoute.getTotalLength();
                
                if(navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate([200, 100, 200]);
                showToast("Laxmikant Heavy Transport Dispatched.");

                deliveryTimer = setInterval(() => {
                    deliveryProgress += 0.005; // Speed
                    
                    if(deliveryProgress >= 1) {
                        clearInterval(deliveryTimer);
                        isDelivering = false;
                        showToast("Equipment safely delivered to Venue.");
                        if(engineOn) enginePlay('djHorn'); // Success sound
                        return;
                    }
                    
                    // Get coordinates along the SVG path
                    const point = deliveryRoute.getPointAtLength(deliveryProgress * pathLength);
                    tractor.style.left = `${point.x}px`;
                    tractor.style.top = `${point.y}px`;
                    
                    // Update Fake ETA
                    const minsLeft = Math.floor((1 - deliveryProgress) * 45); // Fake 45 min trip
                    document.getElementById('etaTracker').innerText = `T-MINUS ${minsLeft}m`;
                    
                }, 50); // 50ms update
            }
        </script>

        <style>
            .bass-drop-wrapper {
                background: #000;
                border: 1px solid #111;
                border-radius: var(--border-radius-lg);
                margin-top: 60px;

            .nuke-button {
                width: 150px;
                height: 150px;
                border-radius: 50%;

                border: 8px solid #222;
                box-shadow:

                    inset 0 10px 20px rgba(255,255,255,0.3),
                    inset 0 -10px 20px rgba(0,0,0,0.8),
                    0 0 0 15px #0a0a0a;
                cursor: pointer;
