                    0 5px 15px rgba(255,0,0,0.5),
                    inset 0 2px 5px rgba(255,255,255,0.1),
                    inset 0 -5px 10px rgba(0,0,0,0.8),
                    0 0 0 15px #0a0a0a;
            }

            /* Cinematic Overlay activated during the sequence */
            #dropOverlay {
                position: fixed; inset: 0; background: rgba(0,0,0,0.9); z-index: 99998;
                display: none; justify-content: center; align-items: center; flex-direction: column;
                opacity: 0; transition: opacity 1s;
            }
            .drop-timer {
                font-family: 'Orbitron'; font-size: 150px; font-weight: 900; color: #ff3333;
                text-shadow: 0 0 50px #ff3333;
            }
            
            /* The intense screen shake class */
            @keyframes apocalypseShake {
                0% { transform: translate(10px, 10px) rotate(0deg); }
                10% { transform: translate(-10px, -20px) rotate(-1deg); }
                20% { transform: translate(-30px, 0px) rotate(1deg); }
                30% { transform: translate(30px, 20px) rotate(0deg); }
                40% { transform: translate(10px, -10px) rotate(1deg); }
                50% { transform: translate(-10px, 20px) rotate(-1deg); }
                60% { transform: translate(-30px, 10px) rotate(0deg); }
                70% { transform: translate(30px, 10px) rotate(-1deg); }
                80% { transform: translate(-10px, -10px) rotate(1deg); }
                90% { transform: translate(10px, 20px) rotate(0deg); }
                100% { transform: translate(0, 0) rotate(0deg); }
            }
            .apocalypse-mode { animation: apocalypseShake 0.1s infinite; filter: contrast(1.5) saturate(1.5); }
        </style>

        <div class="showcase-container reveal-on-scroll">
            <h2 class="section-label-pro"><i class="fas fa-radiation"></i> MAXIMUM OVERDRIVE</h2>
            <p style="text-align: center; color: var(--text-sub); font-family: 'Outfit'; font-size: 13px; margin-top:-15px;">Warning: Initiates the Zero-Gravity Bass Drop Protocol.</p>

            <div class="bass-drop-wrapper">
                <div style="position:absolute; top:20px; left:20px; color:#ff3333; font-family:'Orbitron'; font-size:12px; animation:blinkDot 1s infinite;">SYS. UNLOCKED</div>
                <div class="nuke-button" onclick="initiateBassDrop()">DROP</div>
            </div>
        </div>

        <div id="dropOverlay">
            <div class="drop-timer" id="dropCountdown">3</div>
            <div style="color:#fff; font-family:'Rajdhani'; font-size:20px; letter-spacing:10px; margin-top:20px;">SYSTEM OVERLOAD IMMINENT</div>
        </div>

        <script>
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // XX. CSS 3D Structural Rig Orbit Logic
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            const stage3dEnv = document.getElementById('stage3dEnv');
            const stage3dRig = document.getElementById('stage3dRig');
            const orbitDegDisp = document.getElementById('orbitDeg');
            
            let is3dDragging = false;
            let s3StartX, s3StartY;
            let currentRotX = -15; // Match CSS initial
            let currentRotY = 45;

            stage3dEnv.addEventListener('mousedown', s3DragStart);
            stage3dEnv.addEventListener('touchstart', s3DragStart, {passive: false});

            function s3DragStart(e) {
                is3dDragging = true;
                if(e.type === 'touchstart') e.preventDefault();
                s3StartX = e.type.includes('touch') ? e.touches[0].clientX : e.clientX;
                s3StartY = e.type.includes('touch') ? e.touches[0].clientY : e.clientY;
                stage3dRig.style.transition = 'none';
            }

            window.addEventListener('mousemove', s3DragMove);
            window.addEventListener('touchmove', s3DragMove, {passive: false});

            function s3DragMove(e) {
                if(!is3dDragging) return;
                e.preventDefault();

                const x = e.type.includes('touch') ? e.touches[0].clientX : e.clientX;
                const y = e.type.includes('touch') ? e.touches[0].clientY : e.clientY;

                const deltaX = x - s3StartX;
                const deltaY = y - s3StartY;

                // Map drag to rotation (X drag rotates Y axis, Y drag rotates X axis)
                currentRotY += deltaX * 0.5;
                currentRotX -= deltaY * 0.5;

                // Clamp X rotation to prevent flipping upside down completely
                if(currentRotX > 45) currentRotX = 45;
                if(currentRotX < -80) currentRotX = -80;

                stage3dRig.style.transform = `rotateX(${currentRotX}deg) rotateY(${currentRotY}deg)`;
                orbitDegDisp.innerText = `Y: ${Math.round(currentRotY)}° | X: ${Math.round(currentRotX)}°`;

                s3StartX = x;
                s3StartY = y;
            }

            window.addEventListener('mouseup', s3DragEnd);
            window.addEventListener('touchend', s3DragEnd);

            function s3DragEnd() {
                if(!is3dDragging) return;
                is3dDragging = false;
                stage3dRig.style.transition = 'transform 0.1s ease-out';
            }

            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // YY. Intelligent Graphic EQ Logic
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            function drawEqTarget() {
                const svg = document.getElementById('eqTargetSvg');
                const path = document.getElementById('eqTargetPath');
                const sliders = document.querySelectorAll('.eq-slider');
                const w = svg.clientWidth;
                const h = 200; // Hardcoded height
                
                let d = "";
                const step = w / (sliders.length + 1);

                sliders.forEach((slider, i) => {
                    const targetPct = parseInt(slider.getAttribute('data-target'));
                    const x = step * (i + 1);
                    // Map 0-100% to Y coordinate (0% is bottom/h, 100% is top/0)
                    const y = h - ((targetPct / 100) * h);
                    
                    if(i === 0) d += `M ${x} ${y} `;
                    else d += `L ${x} ${y} `;
                });

                path.setAttribute('d', d);
            }

            function calcEQScore() {
                const sliders = document.querySelectorAll('.eq-slider');
                let totalDiff = 0;
                
                sliders.forEach(slider => {
                    const val = parseInt(slider.value);
                    const target = parseInt(slider.getAttribute('data-target'));
                    totalDiff += Math.abs(val - target);
                });

                // Max possible diff is 100 per slider (100 * 10 = 1000)
                const maxDiff = 1000;
                let accuracy = 100 - ((totalDiff / maxDiff) * 100);
                if(accuracy < 0) accuracy = 0;

                const scoreDisp = document.getElementById('eqScoreDisplay');
                scoreDisp.innerText = `${Math.round(accuracy)}%`;

                if(accuracy > 95) {
                    scoreDisp.style.color = '#00ff00';
                    scoreDisp.style.textShadow = '0 0 20px #00ff00';
                    // Unlock trigger
                    if(typeof playTap === 'function' && scoreDisp.getAttribute('data-unlocked') !== 'true') {
                        scoreDisp.setAttribute('data-unlocked', 'true');
                        showToast("Acoustic Perfection Achieved! System Calibrated.");
                        if(window.engineOn) window.enginePlay('chord1');
                    }
                } else if(accuracy > 70) {
                    scoreDisp.style.color = 'var(--gold-primary)';
                    scoreDisp.style.textShadow = 'none';
                    scoreDisp.removeAttribute('data-unlocked');
                } else {
                    scoreDisp.style.color = '#ff3333';
                    scoreDisp.style.textShadow = 'none';
                    scoreDisp.removeAttribute('data-unlocked');
                }
            }

            // Init SVG drawing
            setTimeout(drawEqTarget, 500);
            window.addEventListener('resize', drawEqTarget);

            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // ZZ. Zero-Gravity Bass Drop Protocol (Cinematic Web Audio)
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            let isDropping = false;
            let dropAudioCtx = null;

            async function initiateBassDrop() {
                if(isDropping) return;
                isDropping = true;
                
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();

                const overlay = document.getElementById('dropOverlay');
                const timer = document.getElementById('dropCountdown');
                
                overlay.style.display = 'flex';
                // Trigger reflow
                void overlay.offsetWidth;
                overlay.style.opacity = '1';

                // Initialize Audio Context securely
                try {
                    const AudioContext = window.AudioContext || window.webkitAudioContext;
                    dropAudioCtx = new AudioContext();
                    
                    // The Riser Sound
                    const rOsc = dropAudioCtx.createOscillator();
                    const rGain = dropAudioCtx.createGain();
                    rOsc.type = 'sawtooth';
                    rOsc.frequency.setValueAtTime(50, dropAudioCtx.currentTime);
                    rOsc.frequency.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(800, dropAudioCtx.currentTime + 3);
                    
                    rOsc.connect(rGain);
                    rGain.connect(dropAudioCtx.destination);
                    
                    rGain.gain.setValueAtTime(0.1, dropAudioCtx.currentTime);
                    rGain.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(1.0, dropAudioCtx.currentTime + 3);
                    
                    rOsc.start();
                    rOsc.stop(dropAudioCtx.currentTime + 3);

                } catch(e) { console.log("Audio API blocked, proceeding visually."); }

                // Countdown Logic
                let count = 3;
                timer.innerText = count;
                if(navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate(100);

                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    count--;
                    if(count > 0) {
                        timer.innerText = count;
                        if(navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate(100);
                    } else {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        executeTheDrop();
                    }
                }, 1000);
            }

            function executeTheDrop() {
                const timer = document.getElementById('dropCountdown');
                timer.innerText = "BOOM";
                timer.style.color = "#fff";
                timer.style.textShadow = "0 0 100px #fff";

                // Physical Screen Shake
                document.body.classList.add('apocalypse-mode');
                
                // Heavy Haptic
                if(navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate([500, 100, 500, 100, 800]);

                // The Bass Impact Audio
                if(dropAudioCtx) {
                    const bOsc = dropAudioCtx.createOscillator();
                    const bGain = dropAudioCtx.createGain();
                    bOsc.type = 'sine';
                    bOsc.frequency.setValueAtTime(120, dropAudioCtx.currentTime);
                    bOsc.frequency.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(20, dropAudioCtx.currentTime + 2);
                    
                    // Add distortion/noise
                    const distNode = dropAudioCtx.createWaveShaper();
                    distNode.curve = makeDistortionCurve(100); // Re-using func from part 13
                    
                    bOsc.connect(distNode);
                    distNode.connect(bGain);
                    bGain.connect(dropAudioCtx.destination);
                    
                    bGain.gain.setValueAtTime(2.0, dropAudioCtx.currentTime);
                    bGain.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.01, dropAudioCtx.currentTime + 2);
                    
                    bOsc.start();
                    bOsc.stop(dropAudioCtx.currentTime + 2);
                }

                // Cleanup & Reset after 2.5 seconds
                setTimeout(() => {
                    document.body.classList.remove('apocalypse-mode');
                    const overlay = document.getElementById('dropOverlay');
                    overlay.style.opacity = '0';
                    setTimeout(() => { 
                        overlay.style.display = 'none'; 
                        isDropping = false;
                        timer.style.color = "#ff3333";
                        timer.style.textShadow = "0 0 50px #ff3333";
                    }, 1000);
                }, 2500);
            }
            
            // Helper for Bass Drop Distortion
            function makeDistortionCurve(amount) {
                const k = typeof amount === 'number' ? amount : 50;
                const n_samples = 44100;
                const curve = new Float32Array(n_samples);
                const deg = Math.PI / 180;
                for (let i = 0; i < n_samples; ++i) {
                    const x = i * 2 / n_samples - 1;
                    curve[i] = (3 + k) * x * 20 * deg / (Math.PI + k * Math.abs(x));
                }
                return curve;
            }
        </script>

        <div class="showcase-container reveal-on-scroll">
            <h2 class="section-label-pro"><i class="fas fa-water"></i> ACOUSTIC INTERFERENCE AI</h2>
            <p style="text-align: center; color: var(--text-sub); font-family: 'Outfit'; font-size: 13px; margin-top:-15px;">Adjust subwoofer distance to visualize the "Power Alley" effect of low frequencies.</p>

            <div class="interference-wrapper">
                <div class="wave-canvas-container">
                    <canvas id="waveCanvas"></canvas>
                    <div class="wave-sub" id="subLeft"></div>
                    <div class="wave-sub" id="subRight"></div>
                    <div style="position:absolute; top:10px; left:50%; transform:translateX(-50%); color:rgba(255,0,0,0.8); font-family:'Orbitron'; font-size:10px; text-shadow: 0 0 5px red; font-weight:bold;">CONSTRUCTIVE INTERFERENCE (POWER ALLEY)</div>
                </div>

                <div class="wave-controls">
                    <div style="display:flex; justify-content:space-between; width:100%; font-family:'Rajdhani'; font-size:12px; color:var(--gold-primary); font-weight:bold;">
                        <span>CLOSER</span><span>SUBWOOFER DISTANCE</span><span>WIDER</span>
                    </div>
                    <input type="range" class="industrial-slider" id="subDistSlider" min="10" max="45" value="20" style="width: 100%;" oninput="updateSubDistance(this.value)">
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>

        <script>
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // AB. Projection Mapping Laser Engine
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            const projCanvas = document.getElementById('projCanvas');
            const pctx = projCanvas.getContext('2d');
            let projPoints = [];
            let isProjDrawing = false;
            let tracerPos = {x: 0, y: 0};
            let tracerTargetIdx = 0;
            let projAnimFrame = null;

            function resizeProj() {
                const rect = projCanvas.parentElement.getBoundingClientRect();
                projCanvas.width = rect.width; projCanvas.height = rect.height;
            }
            window.addEventListener('resize', resizeProj);
            resizeProj();

            function getProjPos(e) {
                const rect = projCanvas.getBoundingClientRect();
                const x = e.type.includes('touch') ? e.touches[0].clientX : e.clientX;
                const y = e.type.includes('touch') ? e.touches[0].clientY : e.clientY;
                return { x: x - rect.left, y: y - rect.top };
            }

            projCanvas.addEventListener('mousedown', startProjDraw);
            projCanvas.addEventListener('touchstart', startProjDraw, {passive: false});

            function startProjDraw(e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                isProjDrawing = true;
                const pos = getProjPos(e);
                projPoints.push(pos);
                document.getElementById('projNodeCount').innerText = projPoints.length;
                
                // If it's the first point, put the tracer there
                if(projPoints.length === 1) {
                    tracerPos.x = pos.x; tracerPos.y = pos.y;
                    if(!projAnimFrame) animateTracer();
                }
            }

            window.addEventListener('mousemove', moveProjDraw);
            window.addEventListener('touchmove', moveProjDraw, {passive: false});

            function moveProjDraw(e) {
                if(!isProjDrawing) return;
                e.preventDefault();
                const pos = getProjPos(e);
                
                // Only add point if moved far enough (performance optimization)
                const lastPoint = projPoints[projPoints.length - 1];
                const dist = Math.hypot(pos.x - lastPoint.x, pos.y - lastPoint.y);
                
                if(dist > 15) {
                    projPoints.push(pos);
                    document.getElementById('projNodeCount').innerText = projPoints.length;
                }
            }

            window.addEventListener('mouseup', () => isProjDrawing = false);
            window.addEventListener('touchend', () => isProjDrawing = false);

            function clearProjection() {
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                projPoints = [];
                tracerTargetIdx = 0;
                pctx.clearRect(0, 0, projCanvas.width, projCanvas.height);
                document.getElementById('projNodeCount').innerText = '0';
            }

            function animateTracer() {
                if(projPoints.length === 0) {
                    projAnimFrame = null;
                    return;
                }
                projAnimFrame = requestAnimationFrame(animateTracer);

                // Fade existing drawing slightly for motion blur
                pctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1)';
                pctx.fillRect(0, 0, projCanvas.width, projCanvas.height);

                // Draw the static wireframe path faintly
                if(projPoints.length > 1) {
                    pctx.beginPath();
                    pctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(184, 41, 255, 0.2)';
                    pctx.lineWidth = 1;
                    pctx.moveTo(projPoints[0].x, projPoints[0].y);
                    for(let i=1; i<projPoints.length; i++) {
                        pctx.lineTo(projPoints[i].x, projPoints[i].y);
                    }
                    // Loop back to start
                    pctx.lineTo(projPoints[0].x, projPoints[0].y);
                    pctx.stroke();
                }

                // Autonomous Laser Tracer Logic
                if(projPoints.length > 1) {
                    const target = projPoints[tracerTargetIdx];
                    const speed = parseInt(document.getElementById('projSpeed').value);
                    
                    const dx = target.x - tracerPos.x;
                    const dy = target.y - tracerPos.y;
                    const dist = Math.hypot(dx, dy);

                    if(dist < speed) {
                        // Reached target, move to next
                        tracerPos.x = target.x;
                        tracerPos.y = target.y;
                        tracerTargetIdx = (tracerTargetIdx + 1) % projPoints.length; // Loop infinitely
                    } else {
                        // Move towards target
                        tracerPos.x += (dx / dist) * speed;
                        tracerPos.y += (dy / dist) * speed;
                    }

                    // Draw glowing laser head
                    pctx.globalCompositeOperation = 'lighter';
                    pctx.beginPath();
                    pctx.arc(tracerPos.x, tracerPos.y, 4, 0, Math.PI * 2);
                    pctx.fillStyle = '#fff';
                    pctx.shadowBlur = 15;
                    pctx.shadowColor = '#b829ff';
                    pctx.fill();
                    pctx.globalCompositeOperation = 'source-over';
                    pctx.shadowBlur = 0; // reset
                }
            }

            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // AC. Tactical Crew Dispatch Logic
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            let activeCrewId = null;
            let activeCrewSkill = null;
            let activeCrewName = null;

            // Base Times (Hours)
            const tasks = {
                tent: { base: 8.0, current: 8.0, element: 'time-tent', bar: 'bar-tent', zone: 'zone-tent' },
                sound: { base: 5.0, current: 5.0, element: 'time-sound', bar: 'bar-sound', zone: 'zone-sound' },
                light: { base: 4.0, current: 4.0, element: 'time-light', bar: 'bar-light', zone: 'zone-light' }
            };

            function selectCrew(id, el) {
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                if(el.classList.contains('assigned')) return; // Already working
                
                document.querySelectorAll('.crew-card').forEach(c => c.classList.remove('selected'));
                el.classList.add('selected');
                
                activeCrewId = id;
                activeCrewSkill = el.getAttribute('data-skill');
                activeCrewName = el.querySelector('.crew-name').innerText;
                
                if(navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate(10);
            }

            function assignToTask(taskId) {
                if(!activeCrewId) {
                    showToast("⚠️ Select a crew member first!");
                    return;
                }
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();

                const task = tasks[taskId];
                
                // Skill Logic: If skill matches task, heavy reduction. Else, minor reduction.
                let reduction = 1.0; // Base 1 hour off
                if(activeCrewSkill === taskId) reduction = 3.0; // Specialist bonus
                if(activeCrewId === 'anil') reduction = 2.0; // Owner bonus applied anywhere
                
                task.current -= reduction;
                if(task.current < 1.0) task.current = 1.0; // Minimum 1 hr
                
                // Update UI
                document.getElementById(task.element).innerText = `${task.current.toFixed(1)} Hrs`;
                document.getElementById(task.bar).style.width = `${(task.current / task.base) * 100}%`;
                
                // Add chip to zone
                const zone = document.getElementById(task.zone);
                if(zone.innerHTML.includes('Tap here')) zone.innerHTML = '';
                zone.innerHTML += `<div class="assigned-chip"><i class="fas fa-check-circle"></i> ${activeCrewName}</div>`;
                
                // Mark crew as assigned
                const crewEl = document.querySelector(`.crew-card[data-id="${activeCrewId}"]`);
                crewEl.classList.remove('selected');
                crewEl.classList.add('assigned');
                
                activeCrewId = null;
                activeCrewSkill = null;
                activeCrewName = null;
                
                calcTotalEta();
            }

            function calcTotalEta() {
                // Tasks happen concurrently (parallel), so total ETA is the max time, not sum.
                const total = Math.max(tasks.tent.current, tasks.sound.current, tasks.light.current);
                const etaEl = document.getElementById('totalEtaTime');
                etaEl.innerText = `${total.toFixed(1)} HRS`;
                
                // Visual pop
                etaEl.style.transform = 'scale(1.2)';
                setTimeout(()=> etaEl.style.transform = 'scale(1)', 200);
            }
            calcTotalEta(); // Init

            function lockLogistics() {
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                showToast("Logistics Plan Locked. Crew Notified.");
                if(navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate([100, 50, 100]);
            }

            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // AD. Acoustic Interference Wave Engine
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            const wCanvas = document.getElementById('waveCanvas');
            const wctx = wCanvas.getContext('2d');
            const subL = document.getElementById('subLeft');
            const subR = document.getElementById('subRight');
            let waveAnimFrame = null;
            let waveTime = 0;
            let subDistPct = 20; // 10 to 45

            function resizeWaveCanvas() {
                const rect = wCanvas.parentElement.getBoundingClientRect();
                wCanvas.width = rect.width; wCanvas.height = rect.height;
            }
            window.addEventListener('resize', resizeWaveCanvas);
            resizeWaveCanvas();

            function updateSubDistance(val) {
                subDistPct = parseInt(val);
                // Center is 50%. Left sub goes left, Right sub goes right.
                subL.style.left = `${50 - subDistPct}%`;
                subR.style.left = `${50 + subDistPct}%`;
                
                // Restart animation if stopped to show changes immediately
                if(!waveAnimFrame) animateWaves();
            }

            function animateWaves() {
                waveAnimFrame = requestAnimationFrame(animateWaves);
                
                wctx.fillStyle = '#000';
                wctx.fillRect(0, 0, wCanvas.width, wCanvas.height);
                
                wctx.globalCompositeOperation = 'screen'; // Crucial for adding light together
                
                waveTime += 1.5; // Speed of expanding rings
                
                // Physical Pixel Coordinates of Subs
                const pxLeft = wCanvas.width * ((50 - subDistPct) / 100);
                const pxRight = wCanvas.width * ((50 + subDistPct) / 100);
                const py = wCanvas.height - 20; // Match CSS bottom: 20px

                wctx.lineWidth = 3;
                wctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(255, 0, 0, 0.4)'; // Red audio waves

                // Draw expanding rings for both subs
                // 15 rings simultaneously
                for(let i=0; i<15; i++) {
                    let r = (waveTime + (i * 30)) % 450; // Radius loops every 450px
                    
                    if(r > 0) {
                        // Fade out as it gets bigger
                        const opacity = 1 - (r / 450);
                        wctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(255, 0, 0, ${opacity * 0.5})`;
                        
                        // Left Sub
                        wctx.beginPath();
                        wctx.arc(pxLeft, py, r, Math.PI, Math.PI * 2); // Only draw top half of circle
                        wctx.stroke();
                        
                        // Right Sub
                        wctx.beginPath();
                        wctx.arc(pxRight, py, r, Math.PI, Math.PI * 2);
                        wctx.stroke();
                    }
                }
                
                wctx.globalCompositeOperation = 'source-over';
                
                // Draw a faint center line to show the "Power Alley"
                wctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(255, 255, 0, 0.2)';
                wctx.lineWidth = 1;
                wctx.beginPath();
                wctx.moveTo(wCanvas.width/2, 0);
                wctx.lineTo(wCanvas.width/2, wCanvas.height);
                wctx.stroke();
            }
            
            // Start engine
            animateWaves();
        </script>
        <style>

            }

            .truss-warning .l-val { color: #ff3333 !important; animation: blinkDot 0.5s infinite; text-shadow: 0 0 10px #ff3333; }
            .truss-warning #tPath { stroke: #ff3333 !important; filter: drop-shadow(0 0 5px #ff3333); }
        </style>

        <div class="showcase-container reveal-on-scroll">
            <h2 class="section-label-pro"><i class="fas fa-wave-square"></i> PHASE ALIGNMENT AI</h2>
            <p style="text-align: center; color: var(--text-sub); font-family: 'Outfit'; font-size: 13px; margin-top:-15px;">Tune the digital delay to perfectly overlap the subwoofer sine waves.</p>

            <div class="phase-align-wrapper">
                <div class="phase-display" id="phaseWrap">
                    <canvas id="phaseCanvas"></canvas>
                    <div style="position:absolute; top:10px; left:10px; font-family:'Orbitron'; font-size:9px; color:#00e5ff; z-index:5;">OSC // SUMMATION WAVEFORM</div>
                </div>

                <div class="phase-hud">
                    <div class="p-stat">
                        <span class="p-lbl">SUB A (FIXED)</span>
                        <span class="p-val" style="color:#00e5ff;">0 ms</span>
                    </div>
                    <div class="p-stat">
                        <span class="p-lbl">SUB B (DELAYED)</span>
                        <span class="p-val" id="delayMsVal" style="color:var(--gold-primary);">0 ms</span>
                    </div>
                    <div class="p-stat">
                        <span class="p-lbl">AMPLITUDE</span>
                        <span class="p-val" id="ampVal">100%</span>
                    </div>
                </div>

                <div class="p-knob-container">
                    <span style="font-family:'Rajdhani'; font-size:12px; color:var(--text-main); margin-bottom:10px; font-weight:bold;">DIGITAL DELAY ADJUSTMENT</span>
                    <input type="range" class="industrial-slider" id="phaseSlider" min="0" max="360" value="180" style="width: 100%; max-width: 300px;" oninput="updatePhase(this.value)">
                </div>

                <div class="phase-status-text ps-destructive" id="phaseVerdict">
                    DESTRUCTIVE INTERFERENCE: BASS CANCELLATION DETECTED
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>

        <script>
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // CC. Kinetic Truss Load Physics Simulator
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            let currentTrussWeight = 0;
            const maxSafeWeight = 600; // kg
            const loadContainer = document.getElementById('hangingLoadsContainer');
            let loadElementsCount = 0;

            function addTrussLoad(type, weight) {
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                
                // Prevent adding too many visually
                if(loadElementsCount >= 6) {
                    showToast("Maximum physical anchor points reached.");
                    return;
                }

                currentTrussWeight += weight;
                loadElementsCount++;

                // Visual Add
                const loadEl = document.createElement('div');
                loadEl.className = 'hanging-load';
                
                // Distribute evenly along the center 60% of the truss
                // Left offset between 20% and 80%
                const leftPos = 20 + ((80 - 20) / 7) * loadElementsCount; 
                loadEl.style.left = `${leftPos}%`;
                
                // Initial top position (will be updated by bending math)
                loadEl.style.top = `10px`; 

                let icon = type === 'audio' ? '<i class="fas fa-speaker"></i>' : '<i class="fas fa-lightbulb"></i>';
                loadEl.innerHTML = `<div class="h-chain"></div><div class="h-box">${icon}<br>${weight}kg</div>`;
                
                loadContainer.appendChild(loadEl);
                updateTrussPhysics();
            }

            function resetTruss() {
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                currentTrussWeight = 0;
                loadElementsCount = 0;
                loadContainer.innerHTML = '';
                updateTrussPhysics();
            }

            function updateTrussPhysics() {
                const env = document.getElementById('trussEnv');
                const tSvg = document.getElementById('trussSvg');
                const pathM = document.getElementById('tPath');
                const pathT = document.getElementById('tPathTop');
                const pathB = document.getElementById('tPathBot');
                
                const wDisplay = document.getElementById('tWeightVal');
                const dDisplay = document.getElementById('tDeflectVal');
                const sDisplay = document.getElementById('tStatusVal');

                wDisplay.innerText = currentTrussWeight;

                // Physics Math: Sag/Deflection is roughly proportional to weight.
                // Assuming max bend visually is 50px at max weight.
                let maxVisualBend = 50; 
                let bendAmount = (currentTrussWeight / maxSafeWeight) * maxVisualBend;
                
                // Exaggerate bend if overloaded to look scary
                if(currentTrussWeight > maxSafeWeight) {
                    bendAmount *= 1.5;
                }

                // Update SVG Bezier Curves (Center control point Y goes down)
                // Format: M startX startY Q controlX controlY endX endY
                // SVG width is roughly 400. Start is 40, End is 360. Center is 200.
                
                const baseYM = 10;
                const baseYTop = 2;
                const baseYBot = 18;

                // Control point is pulled down by bendAmount
                pathM.setAttribute('d', `M 40 ${baseYM} Q 200 ${baseYM + bendAmount * 2} 360 ${baseYM}`);
                pathT.setAttribute('d', `M 40 ${baseYTop} Q 200 ${baseYTop + bendAmount * 2} 360 ${baseYTop}`);
                pathBot.setAttribute('d', `M 40 ${baseYBot} Q 200 ${baseYBot + bendAmount * 2} 360 ${baseYBot}`);

                // Update physical DOM elements hanging on it
                const loads = document.querySelectorAll('.hanging-load');
                loads.forEach(load => {
                    // Approximate position on the curve. Center drops most.
                    const leftPct = parseFloat(load.style.left);
                    // Sine wave approximation for the parabolic curve drop
                    // Map 20-80% to 0-PI. Center (50%) is PI/2 (max value 1).
                    const mappedX = (leftPct - 20) / 60; // 0 to 1
                    const curveMultiplier = Math.sin(mappedX * Math.PI);
                    
                    const dropPx = baseYM + (bendAmount * curveMultiplier);
                    load.style.top = `${dropPx}px`;
                });

                // Real-world millimeter deflection calculation (Fake metric for realism)
                const mmDeflection = (currentTrussWeight * 0.15).toFixed(1);
                dDisplay.innerText = mmDeflection;

                // Warning States
                if(currentTrussWeight > maxSafeWeight) {
                    env.classList.add('truss-warning');
                    sDisplay.innerText = "CRITICAL";
                    sDisplay.style.color = "#ff3333";
                    if(navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate([300, 100, 300]);
                    if(engineOn) enginePlay('impact');
                } else if(currentTrussWeight > maxSafeWeight * 0.8) {
                    env.classList.remove('truss-warning');
                    sDisplay.innerText = "HEAVY LOAD";
                    sDisplay.style.color = "var(--gold-primary)";
                    wDisplay.style.color = "var(--gold-primary)";
                } else {
                    env.classList.remove('truss-warning');
                    sDisplay.innerText = "SAFE";
                    sDisplay.style.color = "#888";
                    wDisplay.style.color = "#00ff00";
                }
            }
            
            // Initialize on load
            setTimeout(updateTrussPhysics, 500);

            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // DD. Volumetric Fog & Laser Fluid Simulator
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            const fCanvas = document.getElementById('fogCanvas');
            const fCtx = fCanvas.getContext('2d');
            let fogParticles = [];
            let fogAnimFrame = null;
            let windSpeedX = 0;
            let targetDensity = 50;

            function initFog() {
                const rect = fCanvas.parentElement.getBoundingClientRect();
                fCanvas.width = rect.width; fCanvas.height = rect.height;
                createFogParticles();
                if(!fogAnimFrame) animateFog();
            }
            window.addEventListener('resize', initFog);
            
            function updateFogParams() {
                targetDensity = parseInt(document.getElementById('fogDensity').value);
                windSpeedX = parseFloat(document.getElementById('fogWind').value);
                createFogParticles(); // Adjust particle count live
            }

            class FogParticle {
                constructor() {
                    this.reset();
                    // Randomize initial Y to fill screen instantly
                    this.y = Math.random() * fCanvas.height; 
                }
                reset() {
                    this.x = Math.random() * fCanvas.width;
                    this.y = fCanvas.height + 20; // Start below screen
                    this.vx = Math.random() * 0.5 - 0.25;
                    this.vy = -(Math.random() * 1 + 0.2); // Float up slowly
                    this.radius = Math.random() * 40 + 20;
                    this.opacity = Math.random() * 0.15 + 0.05;
                }
                update() {
                    this.x += this.vx + windSpeedX;
                    this.y += this.vy;
                    // Wrap around smoothly
                    if(this.y < -this.radius) this.reset();
                    if(this.x > fCanvas.width + this.radius) this.x = -this.radius;
                    if(this.x < -this.radius) this.x = fCanvas.width + this.radius;
                }
                draw(ctx) {
                    // Create soft radial gradient for smoke
                    const grad = ctx.createRadialGradient(this.x, this.y, 0, this.x, this.y, this.radius);
                    grad.addColorStop(0, `rgba(200, 200, 200, ${this.opacity})`);
                    grad.addColorStop(1, 'rgba(200, 200, 200, 0)');
                    ctx.fillStyle = grad;
                    ctx.beginPath();
                    ctx.arc(this.x, this.y, this.radius, 0, Math.PI * 2);
                    ctx.fill();
                }
            }

            function createFogParticles() {
                const currentCount = fogParticles.length;
                // Target count (10 to 100 max mapped to density)
                const count = Math.floor(targetDensity); 
                
                if(count > currentCount) {
                    for(let i=0; i < count - currentCount; i++) fogParticles.push(new FogParticle());
                } else if (count < currentCount) {
                    fogParticles.splice(0, currentCount - count);
                }
            }

            function animateFog() {
                fogAnimFrame = requestAnimationFrame(animateFog);
                
                fCtx.fillStyle = '#050505';
                fCtx.fillRect(0,0, fCanvas.width, fCanvas.height);
                
                // Draw Fog (Screen blend mode for realistic light interaction later)
                fCtx.globalCompositeOperation = 'screen';
                fogParticles.forEach(p => { p.update(); p.draw(fCtx); });
                
                // Draw Volumetric Lasers interacting with fog
                fCtx.globalCompositeOperation = 'lighter';
                
                const lasers = [
                    { x: fCanvas.width * 0.2, c: 'rgba(0, 229, 255, 0.4)' },
                    { x: fCanvas.width * 0.5, c: 'rgba(255, 51, 51, 0.4)' },
                    { x: fCanvas.width * 0.8, c: 'rgba(212, 175, 55, 0.4)' }
                ];

                lasers.forEach(l => {
                    // Base laser beam
                    fCtx.beginPath();
                    fCtx.moveTo(l.x, fCanvas.height);
                    fCtx.lineTo(l.x, 0); // Shooting straight up
                    fCtx.lineWidth = 3;
                    fCtx.strokeStyle = l.c;
                    fCtx.shadowBlur = 10;
                    fCtx.shadowColor = l.c;
                    fCtx.stroke();
                    fCtx.shadowBlur = 0; // reset

                    // Collision detection: Make fog glow when laser hits it
                    // Optimization: Only check a few particles near the laser
                    fogParticles.forEach(p => {
                        if(Math.abs(p.x - l.x) < p.radius) {
                            // Particle is intersected by laser line
                            const glowGrad = fCtx.createRadialGradient(l.x, p.y, 0, l.x, p.y, p.radius);
                            // Glow color matches laser, intensity matches particle opacity
                            const rgb = l.c.match(/\d+, \d+, \d+/)[0]; 
                            glowGrad.addColorStop(0, `rgba(${rgb}, ${p.opacity * 2})`);
                            glowGrad.addColorStop(1, `rgba(${rgb}, 0)`);
                            
                            fCtx.fillStyle = glowGrad;
                            fCtx.beginPath();
                            fCtx.arc(l.x, p.y, p.radius, 0, Math.PI*2);
                            fCtx.fill();
                        }
                    });
                });
                
                fCtx.globalCompositeOperation = 'source-over'; // Reset
            }
            
            setTimeout(initFog, 500);

            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // EE. Acoustic Phase Alignment Tool
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            const phCanvas = document.getElementById('phaseCanvas');
            const phCtx = phCanvas.getContext('2d');
            const phWrap = document.getElementById('phaseWrap');
            
            let phaseOffset = 180; // Default out of phase (0 to 360)
            let phAnimFrame = null;
            let phTime = 0;

            function resizePhase() {
                phCanvas.width = phWrap.clientWidth;
                phCanvas.height = phWrap.clientHeight;
            }
            window.addEventListener('resize', resizePhase);
            resizePhase();

            function updatePhase(val) {
                phaseOffset = parseInt(val);
                
                // Map 0-360 degrees to 0-20ms delay roughly
                const msDelay = ((phaseOffset / 360) * 20).toFixed(1);
                document.getElementById('delayMsVal').innerText = `${msDelay} ms`;
            }

            function animatePhase() {
                phAnimFrame = requestAnimationFrame(animatePhase);
                
                // Fade for oscilloscope tail
                phCtx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3)';
                phCtx.fillRect(0,0, phCanvas.width, phCanvas.height);

                phTime += 0.05; // Speed of wave moving
                
                const w = phCanvas.width;
                const h = phCanvas.height;
                const midY = h / 2;
                const amplitude = h * 0.2; // Height of individual waves
                const frequency = 0.03; // Number of waves on screen

                phCtx.lineWidth = 2;

                // Draw Sub A (Fixed Reference) - Cyan
                phCtx.beginPath();
                phCtx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(0, 229, 255, 0.5)';
                for(let x=0; x<w; x+=2) {
                    const y = midY + Math.sin(x * frequency + phTime) * amplitude;
                    if(x===0) phCtx.moveTo(x,y); else phCtx.lineTo(x,y);
                }
                phCtx.stroke();

                // Draw Sub B (Delayed/Phase Shifted) - Gold
                // Convert degrees to radians for offset
                const offsetRad = phaseOffset * (Math.PI / 180);
                phCtx.beginPath();
                phCtx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(212, 175, 55, 0.5)';
                for(let x=0; x<w; x+=2) {
                    const y = midY + Math.sin(x * frequency + phTime + offsetRad) * amplitude;
                    if(x===0) phCtx.moveTo(x,y); else phCtx.lineTo(x,y);
                }
                phCtx.stroke();

                // Draw SUMMATION WAVE (What the audience actually hears) - White/Glowing
                phCtx.beginPath();
                phCtx.lineWidth = 3;
                phCtx.strokeStyle = '#fff';
                phCtx.shadowBlur = 10; phCtx.shadowColor = '#fff';
                
                let maxSumAmp = 0; // Track amplitude for UI
                
                for(let x=0; x<w; x+=2) {
                    const y1 = Math.sin(x * frequency + phTime) * amplitude;
                    const y2 = Math.sin(x * frequency + phTime + offsetRad) * amplitude;
                    const ySum = y1 + y2;
                    
                    // Track max height
                    if(Math.abs(ySum) > maxSumAmp) maxSumAmp = Math.abs(ySum);

                    if(x===0) phCtx.moveTo(x, midY + ySum); else phCtx.lineTo(x, midY + ySum);
                }
                phCtx.stroke();
                phCtx.shadowBlur = 0; // reset

                // Logic & UI Update
                // Max theoretical sum amplitude is amplitude * 2
                const sumPct = Math.round((maxSumAmp / (amplitude * 2)) * 100);
                document.getElementById('ampVal').innerText = `${sumPct}%`;

                const verdict = document.getElementById('phaseVerdict');
                if(sumPct < 20) {
                    verdict.className = 'phase-status-text ps-destructive';
                    verdict.innerText = "DESTRUCTIVE INTERFERENCE: BASS CANCELLATION DETECTED";
                } else if(sumPct > 95) {
                    verdict.className = 'phase-status-text ps-constructive';
                    verdict.innerText = "PERFECT ALIGNMENT: +6dB CONSTRUCTIVE SUMMATION";
                } else {
                    verdict.className = 'phase-status-text';
                    verdict.style.borderColor = 'var(--gold-primary)';
                    verdict.style.color = 'var(--gold-primary)';
                    verdict.style.background = 'rgba(212,175,55,0.1)';
                    verdict.innerText = "PARTIAL ALIGNMENT: COMB FILTERING DETECTED";
                }
            }
            
            setTimeout(animatePhase, 500);
        </script>

        <style>

        <div class="showcase-container reveal-on-scroll">
            <h2 class="section-label-pro"><i class="fas fa-th"></i> HYPER-SYNC SEQUENCER</h2>
            <p style="text-align: center; color: var(--text-sub); font-family: 'Outfit'; font-size: 13px; margin-top:-15px;">Program the DMX grid. Press play to execute actual screen strobes.</p>

            <div class="strobe-sequencer-wrapper">
                <div class="seq-grid" id="seqGrid">
                    <div class="seq-playhead" id="seqHead"></div>
                    <div class="seq-row-lbl ch-red">R</div>
                    <div class="seq-step" data-ch="red" onclick="toggleStep(this)"></div><div class="seq-step active" data-ch="red" onclick="toggleStep(this)"></div><div class="seq-step" data-ch="red" onclick="toggleStep(this)"></div><div class="seq-step" data-ch="red" onclick="toggleStep(this)"></div>
                    <div class="seq-step active" data-ch="red" onclick="toggleStep(this)"></div><div class="seq-step" data-ch="red" onclick="toggleStep(this)"></div><div class="seq-step" data-ch="red" onclick="toggleStep(this)"></div><div class="seq-step" data-ch="red" onclick="toggleStep(this)"></div>
                    
                    <div class="seq-row-lbl ch-grn">G</div>
                    <div class="seq-step" data-ch="grn" onclick="toggleStep(this)"></div><div class="seq-step" data-ch="grn" onclick="toggleStep(this)"></div><div class="seq-step active" data-ch="grn" onclick="toggleStep(this)"></div><div class="seq-step" data-ch="grn" onclick="toggleStep(this)"></div>
                    <div class="seq-step" data-ch="grn" onclick="toggleStep(this)"></div><div class="seq-step" data-ch="grn" onclick="toggleStep(this)"></div><div class="seq-step active" data-ch="grn" onclick="toggleStep(this)"></div><div class="seq-step" data-ch="grn" onclick="toggleStep(this)"></div>

                    <div class="seq-row-lbl ch-blu">B</div>
                    <div class="seq-step active" data-ch="blu" onclick="toggleStep(this)"></div><div class="seq-step" data-ch="blu" onclick="toggleStep(this)"></div><div class="seq-step" data-ch="blu" onclick="toggleStep(this)"></div><div class="seq-step" data-ch="blu" onclick="toggleStep(this)"></div>
                    <div class="seq-step" data-ch="blu" onclick="toggleStep(this)"></div><div class="seq-step active" data-ch="blu" onclick="toggleStep(this)"></div><div class="seq-step" data-ch="blu" onclick="toggleStep(this)"></div><div class="seq-step" data-ch="blu" onclick="toggleStep(this)"></div>

                    <div class="seq-row-lbl ch-wht">W</div>
                    <div class="seq-step" data-ch="wht" onclick="toggleStep(this)"></div><div class="seq-step" data-ch="wht" onclick="toggleStep(this)"></div><div class="seq-step" data-ch="wht" onclick="toggleStep(this)"></div><div class="seq-step active" data-ch="wht" onclick="toggleStep(this)"></div>
                    <div class="seq-step" data-ch="wht" onclick="toggleStep(this)"></div><div class="seq-step" data-ch="wht" onclick="toggleStep(this)"></div><div class="seq-step" data-ch="wht" onclick="toggleStep(this)"></div><div class="seq-step active" data-ch="wht" onclick="toggleStep(this)"></div>
                </div>

                <div class="seq-controls">
                    <div style="display:flex; align-items:center; gap:10px;">
                        <span style="font-family:'Rajdhani'; color:#aaa; font-size:12px; font-weight:bold;">BPM</span>
                        <input type="number" id="seqBpm" class="bpm-input" value="128">
                    </div>
                    <button class="f-btn" id="btnSeqPlay" style="width:150px; background:var(--gold-primary); color:#000;" onclick="toggleSequencer()">
                        <i class="fas fa-play"></i> EXECUTE
                    </button>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>

        <script>
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // FF. Acoustic Crowd Absorption AI
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            const cCanvas = document.getElementById('crowdCanvas');
            const cCtx = cCanvas.getContext('2d');
            const cWrap = document.getElementById('crowdWrap');
            
            let crowdMode = 'high'; // 'high' or 'low'
            let crowdDensity = 80;
            let crowdDots = [];
            let cAnimFrame = null;
            let cTime = 0;

            function resizeCrowd() {
                cCanvas.width = cWrap.clientWidth;
                cCanvas.height = cWrap.clientHeight;
                generateCrowd();
            }
            window.addEventListener('resize', resizeCrowd);

            function setCrowdFreq(mode, el) {
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                document.querySelectorAll('.freq-btn').forEach(btn => btn.classList.remove('active'));
                el.classList.add('active');
                crowdMode = mode;
                
                const txt = document.getElementById('crowdStatusTxt');
                if(mode === 'high') {
                    txt.innerText = "HIGH-FREQ WAVES (VOCALS)";
                    txt.style.color = "#00e5ff";
                    txt.style.borderColor = "#00e5ff";
                } else {
                    txt.innerText = "LOW-FREQ WAVES (SUB-BASS)";
                    txt.style.color = "#ff3333";
                    txt.style.borderColor = "#ff3333";
                }
            }

            function updateCrowdDensity() {
                crowdDensity = parseInt(document.getElementById('crowdDensitySlider').value);
                generateCrowd();
            }

            function generateCrowd() {
                crowdDots = [];
                // Distribute crowd in the right 70% of the canvas
                const startX = cCanvas.width * 0.3;
                for(let i=0; i<crowdDensity; i++) {
                    crowdDots.push({
                        x: startX + Math.random() * (cCanvas.width - startX - 20),
                        y: Math.random() * cCanvas.height,
                        radius: Math.random() * 2 + 2
                    });
                }
            }

            function animateCrowdAI() {
                cAnimFrame = requestAnimationFrame(animateCrowdAI);
                cTime += 0.05;

                // Motion Blur
                cCtx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.2)';
                cCtx.fillRect(0,0, cCanvas.width, cCanvas.height);

                // Draw Crowd
                cCtx.fillStyle = '#555';
                crowdDots.forEach(dot => {
                    cCtx.beginPath(); cCtx.arc(dot.x, dot.y, dot.radius, 0, Math.PI*2); cCtx.fill();
                });

                // Draw Waves from Speaker (Left side)
                const speakerX = 30;
                const waveCount = crowdMode === 'high' ? 8 : 4; // High freq = more waves, Low = fewer thick waves
                const speed = crowdMode === 'high' ? 3 : 1.5;
                const color = crowdMode === 'high' ? 'rgba(0, 229, 255, 0.6)' : 'rgba(255, 51, 51, 0.8)';
                
                cCtx.lineWidth = crowdMode === 'high' ? 1 : 5;
                cCtx.strokeStyle = color;

                for(let i=0; i<waveCount; i++) {
                    // Calculate radius expanding outwards
                    let r = ((cTime * 40 * speed) + (i * (cCanvas.width/waveCount))) % cCanvas.width;
                    
                    if(r > 0) {
                        // Absorption Logic
                        let opacity = 1.0;
                        if(crowdMode === 'high' && r > cCanvas.width * 0.3) {
                            // High frequencies die off fast in the crowd
                            // Calculate depth into crowd
                            let depth = (r - (cCanvas.width * 0.3)) / (cCanvas.width * 0.7);
                            opacity = 1 - (depth * (crowdDensity / 40)); // More dense = dies faster
                            if(opacity < 0) opacity = 0;
                        } else if (crowdMode === 'low') {
                            // Bass penetrates easily, only natural inverse square dropoff
                            opacity = 1 - (r / cCanvas.width) * 0.3;
                        }

                        if(opacity > 0) {
                            cCtx.globalAlpha = opacity;
                            cCtx.beginPath();
                            cCtx.arc(speakerX, cCanvas.height/2, r, -Math.PI/2.5, Math.PI/2.5); // Arc cone
                            cCtx.stroke();
                        }
                    }
                }
                cCtx.globalAlpha = 1.0;
            }
            
            setTimeout(() => { resizeCrowd(); animateCrowdAI(); }, 500);

            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // GG. Voltage Matrix Chart (Live EKG)
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            const vCanvas = document.getElementById('voltCanvas');
            const vCtx = vCanvas.getContext('2d');
            const vWrap = document.getElementById('voltWrap');
            
            let vData = []; // Array of power values
            let vAnimFrame = null;
            let fuelLevel = 84;
            let engineTemp = 72;

            function resizeVolt() {
                vCanvas.width = vWrap.clientWidth;
                vCanvas.height = vWrap.clientHeight;
                // Pre-fill array with zeros based on width
                vData = new Array(Math.floor(vCanvas.width / 5)).fill(20); 
            }
            window.addEventListener('resize', resizeVolt);

            function animateVoltage() {
                vAnimFrame = requestAnimationFrame(animateVoltage);
                
                // Clear Canvas
                vCtx.clearRect(0,0, vCanvas.width, vCanvas.height);

                // Generate new data point (Base load + random spike)
                // Spikes happen more often if Audio Engine or Sequencer is running
                let newLoad = 40 + (Math.random() * 20 - 10);
                if(window.engineOn && Math.random() > 0.8) newLoad += 30; // Bass hit
                if(isSeqPlaying && Math.random() > 0.5) newLoad += 15; // Strobe hit
                
                // Clamp
                if(newLoad > 95) newLoad = 95;
                if(newLoad < 10) newLoad = 10;

                // Push to array and remove oldest
                vData.push(newLoad);
                vData.shift();

                // Draw Line
                vCtx.beginPath();
                vCtx.strokeStyle = '#00ff00';
                vCtx.lineWidth = 2;
                vCtx.shadowBlur = 10; vCtx.shadowColor = '#00ff00';
                
                const step = vCanvas.width / vData.length;
                
                for(let i=0; i<vData.length; i++) {
                    const x = i * step;
                    // Map 0-100 to canvas height (inverted)
                    const y = vCanvas.height - (vData[i] / 100 * vCanvas.height);
                    if(i===0) vCtx.moveTo(x,y);
                    else vCtx.lineTo(x,y);
                }
                vCtx.stroke();
                vCtx.shadowBlur = 0; // reset
            }

            // Slow Telemetry Update Loop (Fuel/Temp)
            setInterval(() => {
                if(!engineOn && !isSeqPlaying) return; // Only burn fuel if active
                
                fuelLevel -= 0.05;
                engineTemp += (Math.random() * 0.4 - 0.1);
                
                if(fuelLevel < 0) fuelLevel = 0;
                if(engineTemp > 95) engineTemp = 95;
                
                document.getElementById('fuelGauge').innerText = `${fuelLevel.toFixed(0)}%`;
                document.getElementById('fuelBar').style.width = `${fuelLevel}%`;
                
                document.getElementById('tempGauge').innerText = `${engineTemp.toFixed(1)}°C`;
                document.getElementById('tempBar').style.width = `${(engineTemp/120)*100}%`; // Max 120C
                
                // Color warnings
                if(fuelLevel < 20) document.getElementById('fuelBar').style.background = '#ff3333';
                if(engineTemp > 85) document.getElementById('tempBar').style.background = '#ff3333';

            }, 2000);

            setTimeout(() => { resizeVolt(); animateVoltage(); }, 500);

            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // HH. Hyper-Sync Strobe Sequencer
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            let isSeqPlaying = false;
            let currentStep = 0;
            let seqInterval = null;

            function toggleStep(el) {
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                el.classList.toggle('active');
            }

            function toggleSequencer() {
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                const btn = document.getElementById('btnSeqPlay');
                const head = document.getElementById('seqHead');
                
                if(!isSeqPlaying) {
                    isSeqPlaying = true;
                    btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-stop"></i> HALT';
                    btn.style.background = '#ff3333';
                    btn.style.color = '#fff';
                    head.style.display = 'block';
                    currentStep = 0;
                    
                    // BPM Math: 1 min = 60000ms. Length of beat = 60000/BPM.
                    // We are stepping 8th notes, so divide by 2.
                    let bpm = parseInt(document.getElementById('seqBpm').value) || 128;
                    let intervalMs = (60000 / bpm) / 2; 
                    
                    seqInterval = setInterval(runSequencerStep, intervalMs);
                    
                } else {
                    isSeqPlaying = false;
                    btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-play"></i> EXECUTE';
                    btn.style.background = 'var(--gold-primary)';
                    btn.style.color = '#000';
                    head.style.display = 'none';
                    clearInterval(seqInterval);
                    document.body.className = ''; // Clear all flashes
                }
            }

            function runSequencerStep() {
                // Total 8 steps
                currentStep = currentStep % 8;
                
                const head = document.getElementById('seqHead');
                // Calculate physical position of playhead
                // Grid has 40px label + gap, then 8 fractions
                const totalWidth = document.getElementById('seqGrid').clientWidth - 45; 
                const stepWidth = totalWidth / 8;
                head.style.left = `calc(40px + 5px + ${currentStep * stepWidth}px + ${stepWidth/2}px)`;

                // Read Grid data for current column
                // Get all steps, filter by column (index % 8 === currentStep)
                const allSteps = document.querySelectorAll('.seq-step');
                
                let r=false, g=false, b=false, w=false;
                
                // Row 1 (Red) is indices 0-7. Row 2 (Grn) is 8-15.
                if(allSteps[currentStep].classList.contains('active')) r = true;
                if(allSteps[currentStep + 8].classList.contains('active')) g = true;
                if(allSteps[currentStep + 16].classList.contains('active')) b = true;
                if(allSteps[currentStep + 24].classList.contains('active')) w = true;

                // Apply CSS Flash
                // Clear old
                document.body.className = ''; 
                
                // Priority: White > Red > Blue > Green (simplistic mixing)
                if(w) { document.body.classList.add('flash-wht'); if(engineOn) enginePlay('laserA'); }
                else if(r) document.body.classList.add('flash-red');
                else if(b) document.body.classList.add('flash-blu');
                else if(g) document.body.classList.add('flash-grn');

                // Clear flash quickly to create strobe effect
                setTimeout(() => {
                    if(isSeqPlaying) document.body.className = '';
                }, 50); // Flash duration

                currentStep++;
            }
        </script>
        <style>

        <div class="showcase-container reveal-on-scroll">
            <h2 class="section-label-pro"><i class="fas fa-wind"></i> CRYO-JET CO2 CANNON</h2>
            <p style="text-align: center; color: var(--text-sub); font-family: 'Outfit'; font-size: 13px; margin-top:-15px;">Hold to detonate heavy atmospheric CO2 blasts.</p>

                    <i class="fas fa-snowflake"></i> BLAST

        <script>
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // II. AI Auto-BPM Tap Engine
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            let tapTimes = [];
            const btnTap = document.getElementById('btnBpmTap');
            const dispBpm = document.getElementById('bpmDisplay');
            const dispMs = document.getElementById('msPerBeat');
            const waveBg = document.getElementById('bpmWaveBg');
            const syncStatus = document.getElementById('syncStatus');

            btnTap.addEventListener('mousedown', handleTap);
            btnTap.addEventListener('touchstart', (e) => { e.preventDefault(); handleTap(); }, {passive: false});

            function handleTap() {
                const now = Date.now();
                
                // Visual feedback
                btnTap.classList.add('tapped');
                setTimeout(() => btnTap.classList.remove('tapped'), 50);
                if(navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate(15);

                // If it's been more than 2 seconds since last tap, reset array
                if (tapTimes.length > 0 && now - tapTimes[tapTimes.length - 1] > 2000) {
                    tapTimes = [];
                }

                tapTimes.push(now);

                if (tapTimes.length > 1) {
                    // Keep only the last 8 taps for accurate running average
                    if (tapTimes.length > 8) tapTimes.shift();

                    let intervals = [];
                    for (let i = 1; i < tapTimes.length; i++) {
                        intervals.push(tapTimes[i] - tapTimes[i - 1]);
                    }

                    // Average interval in milliseconds
                    const avgInterval = intervals.reduce((a, b) => a + b) / intervals.length;
                    
                    // Convert to BPM (60000 ms per minute)
                    const bpm = Math.round(60000 / avgInterval);

                    // Update UI
                    dispBpm.innerText = bpm;
                    dispMs.innerText = `${Math.round(avgInterval)}ms`;
                    
                    // Adjust background wave density visually based on speed
                    const waveSize = Math.max(5, 30 - (bpm / 10)); // Faster = tighter lines
                    waveBg.style.backgroundSize = `${waveSize}px 100%`;

                    syncStatus.innerText = "CALCULATING...";
                    syncStatus.style.color = "var(--gold-primary)";

                    clearTimeout(window.bpmSyncTimeout);
                    window.bpmSyncTimeout = setTimeout(() => {
                        syncStatus.innerText = "LOCKED";
                        syncStatus.style.color = "#00ff00";
                        
                        // Hook into sequencer if it's running (from Part 26)
                        const seqBpmInput = document.getElementById('seqBpm');
                        if(seqBpmInput) seqBpmInput.value = bpm;
                        
                    }, 1000);
                }
            }

            function resetBpm() {
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                tapTimes = [];
                dispBpm.innerText = "---";
                dispMs.innerText = "---";
                waveBg.style.backgroundSize = "20px 100%";
                syncStatus.innerText = "STANDBY";
                syncStatus.style.color = "#888";
            }

            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // JJ. 3D Laser Tunnel (Wormhole Engine)
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            const tCanvas = document.getElementById('tunnelCanvas');
            const tCtx = tCanvas.getContext('2d');
            const tWrap = document.getElementById('tunnelWrap');
            
            let tunnelColor = '#00e5ff';
            let tAnimFrame = null;
            let tRings = [];
            let tRotation = 0;

            function resizeTunnel() {
                tCanvas.width = tWrap.clientWidth;
                tCanvas.height = tWrap.clientHeight;
            }
            window.addEventListener('resize', resizeTunnel);

            function setTunnelColor(hex, el) {
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                document.querySelectorAll('.t-color-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
                el.classList.add('active');
                tunnelColor = hex;
            }

            // A ring consists of multiple points
            class LaserRing {
                constructor(z) {
                    this.z = z; // Depth. 0 is screen, higher is further away
                    this.points = 12; // Octagon/Dodecagon shape
                    this.radius = 200;
                }
                draw(ctx, cx, cy, rotOffset) {
                    // Projection math (Perspective divide)
                    const fov = 300;
                    const scale = fov / (fov + this.z);
                    
                    // Don't draw if behind camera
                    if(scale < 0) return;

                    ctx.beginPath();
                    for(let i=0; i<=this.points; i++) {
                        const angle = (Math.PI * 2 / this.points) * i + rotOffset;
                        // Calculate 3D position
                        const x3d = Math.cos(angle) * this.radius;
                        const y3d = Math.sin(angle) * this.radius;
                        
                        // Project to 2D
                        const x2d = cx + x3d * scale;
                        const y2d = cy + y3d * scale;
                        
                        if(i===0) ctx.moveTo(x2d, y2d);
                        else ctx.lineTo(x2d, y2d);
                    }
                    
                    // Fade out based on distance
                    const alpha = Math.max(0, 1 - (this.z / 1000));
                    ctx.strokeStyle = tunnelColor;
                    ctx.globalAlpha = alpha;
                    
                    // Closer rings are thicker
                    ctx.lineWidth = scale * 3;
                    ctx.shadowBlur = 10 * scale;
                    ctx.shadowColor = tunnelColor;
                    
                    ctx.stroke();
                    ctx.globalAlpha = 1.0;
                    ctx.shadowBlur = 0;
                }
            }

            function initTunnel() {
                resizeTunnel();
                // Create rings spaced out in Z depth
                for(let i=0; i<20; i++) {
                    tRings.push(new LaserRing(i * 50));
                }
                animateTunnel();
            }

            function animateTunnel() {
                tAnimFrame = requestAnimationFrame(animateTunnel);
                
                // Clear with slight trail
                tCtx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3)';
                tCtx.fillRect(0,0, tCanvas.width, tCanvas.height);
                
                const cx = tCanvas.width / 2;
                const cy = tCanvas.height / 2;
                
                tCtx.globalCompositeOperation = 'screen';
                
                // Read slider for speed and direction
                const speedSlider = document.getElementById('tunnelSpeed');
                const speed = speedSlider ? parseInt(speedSlider.value) / 1000 : 0.02;
                tRotation += speed;

                // Move rings towards camera and draw
                for(let i=0; i<tRings.length; i++) {
                    let r = tRings[i];
                    r.z -= 5; // Move closer
                    
                    // If it passes camera, send it to back
                    if(r.z <= -200) {
                        r.z = 800; // Reset depth
                    }
                    
                    r.draw(tCtx, cx, cy, tRotation + (r.z * 0.002)); // Twist effect
                }
                
                tCtx.globalCompositeOperation = 'source-over';
            }
            setTimeout(initTunnel, 500);

            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // KK. Cryo-Jet CO2 Fluid Dynamics Engine
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            const crCanvas = document.getElementById('cryoCanvas');
            const crCtx = crCanvas.getContext('2d');
            const crWrap = document.getElementById('cryoWrap');
            
            let isCryoActive = false;
            let cryoParticles = [];
            let crAnimFrame = null;

            function resizeCryo() {
                crCanvas.width = crWrap.clientWidth;
                crCanvas.height = crWrap.clientHeight;
            }
            window.addEventListener('resize', resizeCryo);
            resizeCryo();

            function startCryo(e) {
                if(e) e.preventDefault();
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                isCryoActive = true;
                
                document.body.classList.add('frozen-screen');
                crWrap.style.animation = 'heavyBassShake 0.1s infinite';
                
                if(navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate(10000); // Continuous vibration
                
                // Blast sound if engine is on
                if(window.engineOn) window.enginePlay('snare2'); 
                
                if(!crAnimFrame) animateCryo();
            }

            function stopCryo(e) {
                if(e) e.preventDefault();
                isCryoActive = false;
                document.body.classList.remove('frozen-screen');
                crWrap.style.animation = 'none';
                if(navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate(0);
            }

            class CO2Particle {
                constructor(cx, cy) {
                    this.x = cx + (Math.random() * 10 - 5);
                    this.y = cy;
                    // High velocity upward
                    this.vy = -(Math.random() * 15 + 10);
                    // Slight spread outward
                    this.vx = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 4;
                    this.radius = Math.random() * 5 + 5;
                    this.life = 1.0;
                    this.decay = Math.random() * 0.03 + 0.01;
                    // CO2 starts dense/small and expands/fades
                }
                update() {
                    this.x += this.vx;
                    this.y += this.vy;
                    // Friction slows it down
                    this.vy *= 0.92;
                    this.vx *= 0.95;
                    // Gravity pulls it down once velocity is lost (CO2 is heavy)
                    this.vy += 0.5;
                    
                    // Expands as it dissipates
                    this.radius += 0.5;
                    this.life -= this.decay;
                }
                draw(ctx) {
                    ctx.globalAlpha = Math.max(0, this.life);
                    ctx.fillStyle = '#ffffff';
                    
                    // Glow effect
                    ctx.shadowBlur = 15;
                    ctx.shadowColor = '#00e5ff';
                    
                    ctx.beginPath();
                    ctx.arc(this.x, this.y, this.radius, 0, Math.PI * 2);
                    ctx.fill();
                    
                    ctx.shadowBlur = 0;
                    ctx.globalAlpha = 1.0;
                }
            }

            function animateCryo() {
                // Keep running to clear particles even after button released
                if(!isCryoActive && cryoParticles.length === 0) {
                    crAnimFrame = null;
                    crCtx.clearRect(0,0, crCanvas.width, crCanvas.height);
                    return;
                }
                crAnimFrame = requestAnimationFrame(animateCryo);

                // Quick fade for thick smoke trails
                crCtx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0, 10, 20, 0.4)';
                crCtx.fillRect(0,0, crCanvas.width, crCanvas.height);

                crCtx.globalCompositeOperation = 'screen';

                // Spawn new particles if active
                if(isCryoActive) {
                    const cx = crCanvas.width / 2;
                    const cy = crCanvas.height;
                    // Spawn many per frame for dense blast
                    for(let i=0; i<15; i++) {
                        cryoParticles.push(new CO2Particle(cx, cy));
                    }
                }

                // Update and draw
                for(let i = cryoParticles.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
                    let p = cryoParticles[i];
                    p.update();
                    p.draw(crCtx);
                    if(p.life <= 0) cryoParticles.splice(i, 1);
                }
                
                crCtx.globalCompositeOperation = 'source-over';
            }
        </script>

        <style>

        <div class="showcase-container reveal-on-scroll">
            <h2 class="section-label-pro"><i class="fas fa-volume-up"></i> SPL STRESS TEST</h2>

                <input type="range" class="shatter-slider" id="splSlider" min="60" max="145" value="60" oninput="checkSplStress(this.value)">

                    <i class="fas fa-tools"></i> REPAIR STRUCTURAL GLASS
                </button>
