        <script>
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // KK. Drone Swarm Choreography AI
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            const swCanvas = document.getElementById('swarmCanvas');
            const swCtx = swCanvas.getContext('2d');
            const swWrap = document.getElementById('swarmWrap');
            let drones = [];
            let swAnimFrame = null;
            const droneCount = 150;

            function resizeSwarm() {
                const rect = swWrap.getBoundingClientRect();
                swCanvas.width = rect.width; swCanvas.height = rect.height;
            }
            window.addEventListener('resize', resizeSwarm);

            class AEDrone {
                constructor(x, y) {
                    this.x = x; this.y = y;
                    this.tx = x; this.ty = y; // Target X, Y
                    this.color = '#00e5ff';
                    this.baseSpeed = Math.random() * 0.05 + 0.02; // Lerp factor
                }
                update() {
                    // Linear interpolation towards target
                    this.x += (this.tx - this.x) * this.baseSpeed;
                    this.y += (this.ty - this.y) * this.baseSpeed;
                    // Add slight hover physics
                    this.x += Math.sin(Date.now() * 0.002 + this.y) * 0.5;
                    this.y += Math.cos(Date.now() * 0.003 + this.x) * 0.5;
                }
                draw(ctx) {
                    ctx.fillStyle = this.color;
                    ctx.shadowBlur = 10; ctx.shadowColor = this.color;
                    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(this.x, this.y, 2, 0, Math.PI*2); ctx.fill();
                    ctx.shadowBlur = 0;
                }
            }

            function initSwarm() {
                resizeSwarm();
                for(let i=0; i<droneCount; i++) {
                    // Start in random positions
                    drones.push(new AEDrone(Math.random() * swCanvas.width, Math.random() * swCanvas.height));
                }
                setSwarmFormation('scatter');
                animateSwarm();
            }

            function setSwarmFormation(shape) {
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                const cw = swCanvas.width;
                const ch = swCanvas.height;
                const cx = cw / 2;
                const cy = ch / 2;

                let color = '#00e5ff';
                if(shape === 'heart') color = '#ff3333';
                if(shape === 'star') color = '#FFD700';
                if(shape === 'mnd') color = '#00ff00';

                drones.forEach((d, i) => {
                    d.color = color;
                    
                    if(shape === 'scatter') {
                        d.tx = Math.random() * cw;
                        d.ty = Math.random() * ch;
                    } 
                    else if (shape === 'heart') {
                        // Heart math equation
                        const t = (i / droneCount) * Math.PI * 2;
                        const scale = 8;
                        const hx = 16 * Math.pow(Math.sin(t), 3);
                        const hy = -(13 * Math.cos(t) - 5 * Math.cos(2*t) - 2 * Math.cos(3*t) - Math.cos(4*t));
                        d.tx = cx + hx * scale;
                        d.ty = cy + hy * scale;
                    }
                    else if (shape === 'star') {
                        // 5 pointed star math
                        const t = (i / droneCount) * Math.PI * 2;
                        const r = (i % 2 === 0) ? 80 : 30; // Alternate radius
                        const px = Math.cos(t) * r;
                        const py = Math.sin(t) * r;
                        d.tx = cx + px; d.ty = cy + py;
                    }
                    else if (shape === 'mnd') {
                        // Divide drones into 3 groups for M, N, D
                        const groupSize = Math.floor(droneCount / 3);
                        const idx = i % groupSize;
                        const section = Math.floor(i / groupSize); // 0=M, 1=N, 2=D
                        
                        const spacing = cw / 4;
                        const offsetX = (section * spacing) + (spacing/2);
                        
                        // Just random clusters in the general area of the letter for performance
                        d.tx = offsetX + (Math.random() * 40 - 20);
                        d.ty = cy + (Math.random() * 80 - 40);
                    }
                });
            }

            function animateSwarm() {
                swAnimFrame = requestAnimationFrame(animateSwarm);
                
                swCtx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4)'; // Motion blur
                swCtx.fillRect(0,0, swCanvas.width, swCanvas.height);
                
                swCtx.globalCompositeOperation = 'lighter';
                drones.forEach(d => { d.update(); d.draw(swCtx); });
                swCtx.globalCompositeOperation = 'source-over';
            }
            setTimeout(initSwarm, 500);

            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // LL. Neural-Net Feedback Matrix
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            const nrBox = document.getElementById('nrBox');
            const revCanvas = document.getElementById('reviewCanvas');
            const rCtx = revCanvas.getContext('2d');
            
            const reviewData = [
                { name: 'Rohan Sharma', loc: 'Deoghar', text: 'The bass from MND is unbelievable. The whole ground was shaking during my Baraat!' },
                { name: 'Priya Singh', loc: 'Banka', text: 'They built a completely waterproof VIP pandal overnight. Extremely professional crew.' },
                { name: 'Amit Verma', loc: 'Katoria', text: 'The DMX laser show turned our reception into a high-end club. Simply amazing.' },
                { name: 'Suresh Das', loc: 'Beltikri', text: 'Laxmikant tractors navigated the worst roads to get the heavy DJ setup to our village on time.' },
                { name: 'Neha Gupta', loc: 'Jamui', text: 'Audio quality was crystal clear. No feedback during speeches, and massive energy during the dance.' }
            ];

            let revNodes = [];
            let rAnimFrame = null;

            class ReviewNode {
                constructor(data) {
                    this.data = data;
                    this.x = Math.random() * (nrBox.clientWidth - 40) + 20;
                    this.y = Math.random() * (nrBox.clientHeight - 40) + 20;
                    this.vx = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 1.5;
                    this.vy = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 1.5;
                    
                    // Create DOM element
                    this.el = document.createElement('div');
                    this.el.className = 'review-node';
                    this.el.onclick = () => openReview(this);
                    nrBox.appendChild(this.el);
                }
                update() {
                    this.x += this.vx; this.y += this.vy;
                    // Bounce off walls
                    if(this.x <= 10 || this.x >= nrBox.clientWidth - 10) this.vx *= -1;
                    if(this.y <= 10 || this.y >= nrBox.clientHeight - 10) this.vy *= -1;
                    
                    // Update DOM pos
                    this.el.style.left = `${this.x}px`;
                    this.el.style.top = `${this.y}px`;
                }
            }

            function initNeuralReviews() {
                revCanvas.width = nrBox.clientWidth;
                revCanvas.height = nrBox.clientHeight;
                
                reviewData.forEach(d => revNodes.push(new ReviewNode(d)));
                animateNeural();
            }

            function animateNeural() {
                rAnimFrame = requestAnimationFrame(animateNeural);
                
                rCtx.clearRect(0,0, revCanvas.width, revCanvas.height);
                
                // Update Physics
                revNodes.forEach(n => n.update());
                
                // Draw connecting lines between close nodes
                rCtx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(212, 175, 55, 0.3)';
                rCtx.lineWidth = 1;
                
                for(let i=0; i<revNodes.length; i++) {
                    for(let j=i+1; j<revNodes.length; j++) {
                        const dx = revNodes[i].x - revNodes[j].x;
                        const dy = revNodes[i].y - revNodes[j].y;
                        const dist = Math.hypot(dx, dy);
                        
                        if(dist < 150) {
                            rCtx.beginPath();
                            rCtx.moveTo(revNodes[i].x, revNodes[i].y);
                            rCtx.lineTo(revNodes[j].x, revNodes[j].y);
                            rCtx.stroke();
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            
            function openReview(nodeObj) {
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                // Reset active states
                document.querySelectorAll('.review-node').forEach(n => n.classList.remove('active'));
                nodeObj.el.classList.add('active');
                
                // Populate popup
                document.getElementById('rcClient').innerText = nodeObj.data.name;
                document.getElementById('rcLoc').innerText = nodeObj.data.loc;
                document.getElementById('rcText').innerText = nodeObj.data.text;
                
                document.getElementById('reviewPopup').classList.add('show');
                
                // Pause animation to let user read
                if(rAnimFrame) { cancelAnimationFrame(rAnimFrame); rAnimFrame = null; }
            }

            function closeReview() {
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                document.getElementById('reviewPopup').classList.remove('show');
                document.querySelectorAll('.review-node').forEach(n => n.classList.remove('active'));
                if(!rAnimFrame) animateNeural();
            }

            window.addEventListener('resize', () => {
                revCanvas.width = nrBox.clientWidth;
                revCanvas.height = nrBox.clientHeight;
            });
            setTimeout(initNeuralReviews, 500);

            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // MM. Acoustic Glass-Shatter Physics Game
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            let isGlassBroken = false;

            function checkSplStress(val) {
                if(isGlassBroken) {
                    // Prevent slider from going down if broken until repaired
                    document.getElementById('splSlider').value = 145;
                    return; 
                }

                const display = document.getElementById('splLevel');
                const env = document.getElementById('shatterEnv');
                const panel = document.getElementById('glassPanel');
                
                display.innerText = `${val} dB`;

                // Audio Context Hook for physical feedback
                if(window.engineOn && window.proCtx) {
                    // Dynamically increase distortion/volume based on slider
                    const norm = (val - 60) / 85; // 0.0 to 1.0
                    window.masterVol.gain.setTargetAtTime(0.8 + (norm * 1.5), window.proCtx.currentTime, 0.1);
                }

                // Shake intensity based on volume
                if(val > 100) {
                    display.style.color = '#ffff00';
                    const shakeAmt = (val - 100) / 10; // 0 to 4.5px
                    panel.style.transform = `translate(${Math.random()*shakeAmt - shakeAmt/2}px, ${Math.random()*shakeAmt - shakeAmt/2}px)`;
                    if(navigator.vibrate && val % 5 === 0) navigator.vibrate(10);
                } else {
                    display.style.color = '#fff';
                    panel.style.transform = 'translate(0, 0)';
                }

                // BREAK POINT (140 dB)
                if(val >= 140) {
                    isGlassBroken = true;
                    env.classList.add('broken');
                    display.innerText = "CRITICAL FAIL";
                    panel.style.transform = 'translate(0, 0)'; // Stop smooth shake
                    
                    // Heavy Haptic & Visual glitch
                    if(navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate([300, 100, 500]);
                    document.body.classList.add('apocalypse-mode');
                    setTimeout(() => document.body.classList.remove('apocalypse-mode'), 200);
                    
                    if(engineOn) enginePlay('impact');
                    
                    document.getElementById('btnRepairGlass').style.display = 'block';
                }
            }

            function repairGlass() {
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                isGlassBroken = false;
                
                const env = document.getElementById('shatterEnv');
                env.classList.remove('broken');
                
                const slider = document.getElementById('splSlider');
                slider.value = 60;
                
                document.getElementById('splLevel').innerText = "60 dB";
                document.getElementById('splLevel').style.color = "#fff";
                document.getElementById('btnRepairGlass').style.display = 'none';
                
                if(window.engineOn && window.proCtx) {
                    window.masterVol.gain.setTargetAtTime(0.8, window.proCtx.currentTime, 0.1);
                }
                
                showToast("Structural Glass Repaired.");
            }
        </script>

        <script>
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // XX. Final Booking Matrix Sync & Submission Logic
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            
            // Sync the budget display continuously
            setInterval(() => {
                const finalCostEl = document.getElementById('matrixFinalCost');
                if(finalCostEl && typeof currentTotalBudget !== 'undefined') {
                    // Pulling from the Dream Crafter Builder variable
                    // If builder is 0, pull from quote engine variable
                    let val = currentTotalBudget > 0 ? currentTotalBudget : (typeof currentTotalQuote !== 'undefined' ? currentTotalQuote : 0);
                    finalCostEl.innerText = `₹${val.toLocaleString()}`;
                }
            }, 1000);

            function submitMasterBooking() {
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                
                const name = document.getElementById('mbName').value.trim();
                const phone = document.getElementById('mbPhone').value.trim();
                const loc = document.getElementById('mbLocation').value.trim();
                const date = document.getElementById('mbDate').value;
                const cost = document.getElementById('matrixFinalCost').innerText;
                const btn = document.getElementById('btnMasterSubmit');

                if(!name || phone.length < 10 || !loc) {
                    showToast("⚠️ ERROR: Name, Valid Phone, and Location are mandatory.");
                    // Shake animation for error
                    btn.style.animation = 'heavyBassShake 0.4s';
                    setTimeout(()=> btn.style.animation = '', 400);
                    return;
                }

                btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-spinner fa-spin"></i> ENCRYPTING CONTRACT...';
                btn.style.pointerEvents = 'none';

                const formattedMsg = `👑 *MND PREMIUM BOOKING SECURED* 👑\n---------------------------\n👤 *Client:* ${name}\n📞 *Phone:* ${phone}\n📍 *Venue:* ${loc}\n📅 *Date:* ${date || 'TBD'}\n💰 *System Est:* ${cost}\n\n⏱️ *Timestamp:* ${new Date().toLocaleString()}\n_Source: Master Booking Matrix V3_`;

                // Uses global Telegram variables
                fetch(`https://api.telegram.org/bot${TG_TOKEN}/sendMessage`, { 
                    method: 'POST', 
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, 
                    body: JSON.stringify({ chat_id: TG_CHAT, text: formattedMsg, parse_mode: 'Markdown' }) 
                })
                .then(res => {
                    if(res.ok) {
                        btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-check-double"></i> CONTRACT LOCKED. WE WILL CALL YOU.';
                        btn.style.background = '#00ff00';
                        btn.style.color = '#000';
                        showToast("Booking received at Beltikri HQ.");
                        if(engineOn) enginePlay('impact'); // Boom sound on success
                    } else { throw new Error('Network fail'); }
                })
                .catch(err => {
                    btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-exclamation-triangle"></i> NETWORK FAIL. TRY AGAIN.';
                    btn.style.background = '#ff3333';
                    btn.style.color = '#fff';
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-satellite-dish"></i> INITIATE BOOKING';
                        btn.style.background = 'linear-gradient(90deg, var(--gold-primary), #ffdf00)';
                        btn.style.color = '#000';
                        btn.style.pointerEvents = 'auto';
                    }, 3000);
                });
            }

            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            // YY. Command Center Logic (Hidden Owner Portal)
            // -------------------------------------------------------------------
            let adminTapCount = 0;
            let adminTapTimer = null;
            let currentPin = "";
            const MASTER_PIN = "2026"; // Default system unlock code

            // Tapping the hidden zone 5 times quickly triggers the login
            function tapAdminTrigger() {
                adminTapCount++;
                clearTimeout(adminTapTimer);
                
                if(adminTapCount >= 5) {
                    if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                    if(navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate([100, 50, 100]);
                    document.getElementById('commandCenter').classList.add('active');
                    adminTapCount = 0;
                }
                
                adminTapTimer = setTimeout(() => { adminTapCount = 0; }, 2000);
            }

            function enterPin(num) {
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                if(currentPin.length < 4) {
                    currentPin += num;
                    updatePinDisplay();
                }
                
                if(currentPin.length === 4) {
                    setTimeout(verifyPin, 300);
                }
            }

            function updatePinDisplay() {
                const screen = document.getElementById('ccPinScreen');
                // Display asterisks for entered digits, underscore for remaining
                let displayStr = "";
                for(let i=0; i<4; i++) {
                    if(i < currentPin.length) displayStr += "*";
                    else displayStr += "_";
                }
                screen.innerText = displayStr;
            }

            function clearPin() {
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                currentPin = "";
                updatePinDisplay();
                document.getElementById('ccPinScreen').style.borderColor = '#00e5ff';
                document.getElementById('ccPinScreen').style.color = '#00e5ff';
            }

            function verifyPin() {
                const screen = document.getElementById('ccPinScreen');
                if(currentPin === MASTER_PIN) {
                    // Success
                    screen.style.borderColor = '#00ff00';
                    screen.style.color = '#00ff00';
                    if(navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate(300);
                    if(window.engineOn) window.enginePlay('laserA');
                    
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        document.getElementById('ccLoginUI').style.display = 'none';
                        document.getElementById('ccDashUI').style.display = 'block';
                        // Start fake live traffic data
                        setInterval(() => {
                            const vis = document.getElementById('fakeVis');
                            let current = parseInt(vis.innerText);
                            current += (Math.random() > 0.5 ? 1 : -1) * Math.floor(Math.random() * 3);
                            if(current < 5) current = 5;
                            vis.innerText = current;
                        }, 4000);
                    }, 500);

                } else {
                    // Fail
                    screen.style.borderColor = '#ff3333';
                    screen.style.color = '#ff3333';
                    screen.style.animation = 'heavyBassShake 0.4s';
                    if(navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate([50, 50, 50, 50]);
                    
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        screen.style.animation = '';
                        clearPin();
                    }, 500);
                }
            }

            function closeCommandCenter() {
                if(typeof playTap === 'function') playTap();
                document.getElementById('commandCenter').classList.remove('active');
                
                // Reset states after animation
                setTimeout(() => {
                    clearPin();
                    document.getElementById('ccLoginUI').style.display = 'block';
                    document.getElementById('ccDashUI').style.display = 'none';
                }, 500);
            }
            
            // Init empty display
            updatePinDisplay();
        </script>
        <script>
            // 1. Advanced Scroll Reveal Engine
            // This observes elements as you scroll down and fades them in smoothly
            document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", () => {
                const observerOptions = {
                    threshold: 0.1, // Trigger when 10% of the element is visible
                    rootMargin: "0px 0px -50px 0px"
                };

                const scrollObserver = new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {
                    entries.forEach(entry => {
                        if (entry.isIntersecting) {
                            // Add 'visible' class to trigger CSS animations
                            entry.target.classList.add('visible');
                            // Stop observing once animated to save CPU
                            scrollObserver.unobserve(entry.target); 
                        }
                    });
                }, observerOptions);

                // Target all containers we built with the reveal class
                document.querySelectorAll('.reveal-on-scroll').forEach(el => {
                    scrollObserver.observe(el);
                });
            });

            // 2. Master Loading Screen Removal
            // We wait for window.load (which means all fonts, images, and scripts are ready)
            window.addEventListener("load", () => {
                const globalLoader = document.getElementById("mndGlobalLoader");
                
                if (globalLoader) {
                    // Fade out
                    globalLoader.style.opacity = "0";
                    globalLoader.style.transition = "opacity 0.8s cubic-bezier(0.25, 1, 0.5, 1)";
                    
                    // Remove from DOM after fade and announce system ready
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        globalLoader.style.display = "none";
                        
                        // Physical feedback that the website is fully loaded
                        if(navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate([100, 50, 100]);
                        
                        // Use the Toast notification system we built in Part 10
                        if(typeof showToast === 'function') {
                            showToast("SYSTEM BOOT COMPLETE. WELCOME TO MND V3.1 PRO.");
                        }
                    }, 800);
                }
            });

            // 3. Global Touch Optimizer for Mobile
            // Prevents the screen from scrolling when the user is trying to use 
            // the DJ Mixer, Laser Canvas, Stage Builder, or Faders.
            const interactiveElements = document.querySelectorAll('canvas, .tap-pad, .fader-input, .sub-sim-wrapper, .scanner-container');
            
            interactiveElements.forEach(el => {
                el.addEventListener('touchmove', function(e) {
                    // Only prevent default if it's a specific interactive canvas or pad
                    // Allows normal scrolling on standard containers
                    if(this.tagName === 'CANVAS' || this.classList.contains('tap-pad') || this.classList.contains('scanner-container')) {
                        e.preventDefault();
                    }
                }, { passive: false }); // Passive false is required to use preventDefault
            });

            // 4. Security Sandbox (Optional - prevents right click/inspect element on mobile)
            // Uncomment the lines below if you want to lock down your code from being copied
            /*
            document.addEventListener('contextmenu', event => event.preventDefault());
            document.onkeydown = function(e) {
                if(e.keyCode == 123) return false; // F12
                if(e.ctrlKey && e.shiftKey && e.keyCode == 'I'.charCodeAt(0)) return false; // Ctrl+Shift+I
                if(e.ctrlKey && e.shiftKey && e.keyCode == 'J'.charCodeAt(0)) return false; // Ctrl+Shift+J
                if(e.ctrlKey && e.keyCode == 'U'.charCodeAt(0)) return false; // Ctrl+U
            }
            */

        </script>
    </body>
</html>
